## lim-blamey-mctypoface.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-blamey-mctypoface.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-blamey-mctypoface.mdx
bytes: 4716
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-blamey-mctypoface
title: Blamey McTypoface
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about blame-shifting, scapegoat logs, and a
  fault-routing analyst who's never once been wrong—just ask him.
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'blame routing, scapegoating, error redirection, passive aggression'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-BLAMEY-MCTYPOFACE"
relatedMascots: ["003.blamey-mctypoface"]
concepts: ["blame-shift", "scapegoat", "fault-routing", "passive-aggressive"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="The Blame Shift" icon="user-x">
"**Well, actually,**" <u>Blamey</u> began,  
"The fault's in your *deployment plan*."  
He pointed at Tim,  
Who pointed at Kim,  
Who pointed at someone who **ran**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Log Obscurity" icon="file-minus">
He filed the blame deep in a log  
Then screwed the intern like a cog.  
"It's not my mistake—  
It's your line that breaks."  
Then he stamped it and hid in the fog.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Buggy Tryst" icon="bug">
Old Blamey once bedded a bug  
And gave it a satisfied shrug.  
"I'll blame it on Dave,  
That cowardly knave,"  
Then pulled the exception to tug.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Scapegoat Registry" icon="book-x">
The scapegoat log grew every night  
With entries both saucy and tight.  
Each record laid bare  
Someone's shame and despair  
While Blamey watched, rigid with spite.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Red Note" icon="sticky-note">
He "NOTED" a ticket in red  
Then took the stack trace back to bed.  
He stroked every line,  
Called the segfault "divine,"  
And blamed Cssandra instead.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Null Exposure" icon="ghost">
A NULL pointer wandered in nude.  
Blamey said, "That's terribly rude."  
He rerouted the shame  
To a different dev's name,  
Then got off on the magnitude.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Triplicate Blame" icon="files">
His triplicate blame forms were thick—  
Each copy more lurid, more slick.  
Department One: "Noted."  
Department Two: "Quoted."  
Department Three: "That's a whole dick."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stamp of Others" icon="stamp">
At three-fourteen AM, barely dressed,  
He stamped "OTHER PEOPLE'S" with zest  
On faults, failures, leaks,  
And someone else's mystiques,  
While the syslog lay bare and impressed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dunce Deployment" icon="graduation-cap">
They said, "Blamey, own it for once."  
He replied with a withering stunts:  
"The error's not mine,  
It's line forty-nine,  
And whoever deployed it's a dunce."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Wrapped Misdirection" icon="gift">
So if blame arrives wrapped in a bow  
And the fault trace has put on a show  
Of misdirection and heat,  
With a red-stamped receipt,  
That's McTypoface—letting you know.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sarcastic Triage" icon="clipboard-list">
"It's obviously your fault," he hissed,  
While ticking your name off his list.  
He stamped it with glee,  
Laughed, "Better you than me,"  
And dismissed it as if it was missed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Red Pen" icon="pen-tool">
He carried a terrible pen,  
And circled the syntax of men.  
"This bracket is flawed!  
Your logic's a fraud!"  
Then he crashed the compiler again.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Infinite Scapegoats" icon="users">
The scapegoats were lined in a row,  
With nowhere to hide and to go.  
Blamey handed them tags,  
Put their careers into bags,  
And smiled at the horror below.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cosmic Ray Excuse" icon="sun">
"It wasn't the code," Blamey lied,  
"A cosmic ray hit from outside."  
The server had burned,  
But Blamey just turned,  
And blamed it on Jupiter's tide.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Bureaucratic Glee" icon="file-signature">
He filed the report in the trash,  
Then demanded a payment in cash.  
"The fault has been found,  
It's nowhere around,"  
He declared with a snide little dash.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Blame Cascade" icon="share-2">
He passed the hot potato along,  
In a chain that grew longer and wrong.  
Each person in line  
Blamed the one who designed  
The system that broke all their song.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Documentation Dodge" icon="document-x">
When asked for the documentation,  
He offered a blameful narration:  
"It's not written down,  
So let's wear the crown,  
Of systematic miscommunication."  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-blinko-chompframe.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-blinko-chompframe.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-blinko-chompframe.mdx
bytes: 3070
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-blinko-chompframe
title: Blinko Chompframe
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about prophetic vending errors, expired fortune
  cards, and a 1993 animatronic snack oracle who was duct-taped into silence.
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: nostalgic
subject: >-
  vending machine, 1993, Grizzly Chomps, animatronic, prophecy, expired snacks,
  gas station
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-BLINKO-CHOMPFRAME"
relatedMascots: ["937.blinko-chompframe"]
concepts: ["vending-machine", "animatronic", "prophecy", "expired-snacks", "1993"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Snack Oracle" icon="monitor">
Blinko emerged from a *Chevron stall*,  
A snack oracle, half-topiary and all.  
His LED face glitched,  
His cupcake was hitched,  
And the vending errors won't forestall.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Snack Fate" icon="file-text">
He dispensed *empty wrappers* with art—  
Poetic misprints from the heart.  
The fortune cards read  
"SOON" (guaranteed),  
And the snack fate was only the start.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Prophecy Nobody Deemed" icon="volume-2">
"*EAT B4 YOU'RE EATEN,*" he screamed  
Through a staticky loop, as he teemed  
With corrupted ZIP codes,  
Outdated chip odes,  
And a prophecy nobody deemed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pump'n'Chug Mystery" icon="fuel">
He was *banned* from three gas station chains  
For hauntings—prophetic refrains  
That chilled every lounge,  
Made the patrons all scrounge,  
And the Pump'n'Chug never explains.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Non-Serviceable Cupcake Grip" icon="hand">
His *cupcake grip* is non-serviceable—  
The foil-wrapped contents: irreversible.  
The paw must retain it,  
No one can explain it,  
And the contents are wholly immersible.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Prophecy Buffering" icon="loader">
Insert *25 cents* and just ask—  
Response may be delayed by the task  
Of prophecy buffering,  
The LED stuttering,  
And the snack-fate oracle's mask.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Jalapeño Future" icon="zap">
"*Jalapeño Future Detected!*"  
He screeched, unprompted, dejected.  
Three fortune cards fell,  
Each reading "SOON"—well,  
The manager unplugged him, deflected.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Grizzly Chomps Skid" icon="timer">
He's *misremembered* by 90s kids  
Who never actually saw his grid-  
ded LED face.  
The promotional race  
Of 1993's Grizzly Chomps skids.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Corroding Animatronic" icon="skull">
He dislikes *modern QR codes*,  
Freshness seals, and the goat who rode  
His replacement throne  
In 2001, alone,  
And the animatronic corrodes.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Broken Marooned Oracle" icon="ghost">
So if fortune cards read just "SOON"  
And the vending machine plays a tune  
Of corrupted fame,  
That's *Blinko's* great claim:  
Half-bitten, fully broken, marooned.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-blue-dreamweaver.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-blue-dreamweaver.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-blue-dreamweaver.mdx
bytes: 3034
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-blue-dreamweaver
title: Blue Dreamweaver
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about berry-mist archives, strain profile chants,
  and an ethereal dispensary curator who misfiled a patient record as 'berry
  poetry.'
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: archival
subject: 'dispensary, Blue Dream, cannabis, berry mist, Hot Springs, Arkansas, medical'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-BLUE-DREAMWEAVER"
relatedMascots: ["207.blue-dreamweaver"]
concepts: ["dispensary", "blue-dream", "cannabis", "berry", "hot-springs"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Berry Mist Phase" icon="wind">
Blue Dreamweaver drifts through the *haze*,  
Weaving berry mists into days  
Of archival calm.  
Her spectral-form balm  
Infuses the metadata's phase.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Berry Poetry Record" icon="file-text">
She misfiled a *patient record* clean  
As "berry poetry"—the serene  
Blurring of data  
With dreamy errata  
Left the compliance auditor keen.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Hazy Filing" icon="cloud">
She overinfused *metadata mist*,  
Clouding archives—no data dismissed,  
But the records turned hazy,  
The filing got lazy,  
And the strain profiles blurred and were kissed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Berry-Dimmed Light" icon="lamp">
She chanted *strain profiles* one night  
During a compliance audit—not right.  
The filings delayed,  
The auditor swayed,  
And the berry mist dimmed every light.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Blue Dream Bouquet" icon="flower">
"*Weave relief, dream in haze,*" she would say,  
While the dispensary hummed through the day.  
Each patient record  
Was tenderly stored  
In the archive's Blue Dream bouquet.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Therapeutic Feat" icon="heart">
Her spectral form trails *berry sweet*  
Through Hot Springs—a therapeutic feat.  
Each file she weaves  
Through cannabis leaves,  
And the archive is almost complete.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Medical Clause Compliance" icon="shield-check">
She maintains *compliance* with laws  
Of Arkansas's medical clause.  
Each strain profile sung  
In the moonlit among  
The archives deserves its applause.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Signature Fiction" icon="pen-tool">
Her dreamy rituals sometimes *blur*  
The lines between data and her  
Poetic conviction  
That metadata's fiction  
Is just Berry Dream's signature.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Hybrid Calm" icon="moon">
Each patient's story she *preserves*  
With therapeutic, berry-scent curves.  
The hybrid calm saved,  
The metadata engraved,  
And the archive serenely observes.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dreamy and Fair" icon="sparkles">
So if berry mists cloud the air  
And the records have poetry flair,  
That's *Blue Dreamweaver*:  
Where the haze is a keeper,  
And the archive is dreamy and fair.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-boily-mcplaterton.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-boily-mcplaterton.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-boily-mcplaterton.mdx
bytes: 4675
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-boily-mcplaterton
title: Boily McPlaterton
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about thermal panic, combustible mascots, and a CPU
  that refuses paste on ideological grounds.
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: thermal
subject: 'overheating, meltdown, thermal panic, legacy hardware, fan failure'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-BOILY-MCPLATERTON"
relatedMascots: ["004.boily-mcplaterton"]
concepts: ["thermal-panic", "overheat", "meltdown", "legacy-hardware"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="The Hot Seat" icon="thermometer-sun">
<u>Old Boily</u> ran *hot* as a whore  
In a **server room** lacking a door.  
His idle was **steaming**,  
His fan RPM *screaming*,  
And his thermal paste? "**Never!**" he swore.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Frying-Pan Plan" icon="flame">
He said, "Why just crash when you can  
Combust like a frying-pan plan?"  
His casing went crack,  
Smoke poured from the back,  
And the room smelled like scorched DigiPan.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Coolant-Free Throttle" icon="gauge">
At two PM daily he'd throttle,  
Then suck from his coolant-free bottle.  
The temps hit one-ten,  
He came hard and then  
Rebooted in loop at full-throttle.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Thermal Midnight" icon="zap">
A thermal spike hit in the night.  
Boily said, "Hold me real tight."  
The legacy board  
Let out a great roar,  
And the firmware came twice before light.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Voltage Instigator" icon="radiation">
He blamed the voltage regulator—  
Said, "That prick is the real instigator."  
But the fan override  
Caught him naked inside,  
Spooned the heat dissipator.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ninety-Three C" icon="thermometer">
"My idle temp's ninety-three C,"  
Boily moaned, "come and sit next to me."  
The heatsink said, "No,  
You burn everything, bro."  
But he mounted it anyway. Whee.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Morse Intercourse" icon="binary">
His bug reports came out in Morse:  
Dot-dash-dot with emotional force.  
The audit assumed  
The whole rack was consumed,  
But it was just Boily's intercourse.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Emergency Cooldown" icon="snowflake">
Emergency Cooldown Form 88-B  
Was filed while he humped the PC.  
The livestream went wild,  
The thermals beguiled,  
And the sysadmin wept openly.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unventilated Fit" icon="wind">
He screeches near unventilated kit,  
A noise somewhere between moan and spit.  
The racks start to sweat,  
The cables get wet,  
And the server room throws a hot fit.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smoke and Bloom" icon="cloud-fog">
So when smoke fills the air and you feel  
A heat that no coldpatch can heal,  
That's Boily in bloom:  
The warmest in the room,  
Getting intimate with every last seal.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Thermal Despair" icon="flame">
Boily stared at the thermostat dial,  
And let out a sulfurous smile.  
"If I burn down the rack,  
There's no going back,"  
He thought, heating up by the mile.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Singed Motherboard" icon="cpu">
The legacy server was old,  
With circuits and pathways of gold.  
Boily melted the frame,  
Said, "It's a crying shame,  
That nobody likes to be cold."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Plastic Perfume" icon="wind">
The scent of hot plastic and wire  
Arose from his digital pyre.  
He fanned it with pride,  
While the cooling fans died,  
And muttered, "I love a good fire."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Panic Mode Engaged" icon="alert-triangle">
The panic loop spun like a top,  
With nowhere to cool down or stop.  
He hit ninety-nine,  
Screamed, "This is divine!"  
And waited for the system to drop.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Liquid Nitrogen Tease" icon="snowflake">
They tried liquid nitrogen spray,  
To coax his high temp down a way.  
He laughed at the frost,  
Said, "Your server is lost,"  
And burned through the coolant all day.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Heat-Induced Cascade" icon="flame-alt">
When the thermals hit one-twenty mark,  
Boily lit up the whole dark.  
Capacitors popped,  
The whole system stopped,  
And circuits went out with a spark.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Melting Point" icon="droplet">
He melted the copper and steel,  
Got off on the molten ideal.  
When the warranty broke,  
He just let out a croak,  
Said, "This is the way I feel."  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-boundary-audit.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-boundary-audit.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-boundary-audit.mdx
bytes: 1588
```markdown
---
title: "Stub: Mascot Boundary Audit"
slug: limericks/lim-boundary-audit
description: >-
  Procedural stub awaiting contextual binding for Mascot Boundary Audit.
date: 2026-06-08T11:27:17.792Z
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: []
concepts: []
family: "other"
---



## Procedural Entry

<Limerick type="danger" title="Procedural Stub" icon="file">
The record is utterly bare,  
With nothing but digital air.  
We printed the form,  
To weather the storm,  
And left it to quietly tear.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="PROCEDURAL_CLEAN" icon="map">
The boundary audit is clear,
The mascot is nowhere near here.
The lines are defined,
And properly signed,
To govern the procedural sphere.
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="caution" title="MISFILED_CONFIDENCE" icon="map">
The boundary lines are immense,
To keep all the cows in the fence.
The mascot is grass,
And sits on its ass,
Without any logical sense.
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="FATIGUE_GOLD_BRICK" icon="map">
The audit of borders is done,
Which really is no kind of fun.
I measure the space,
And cover my face,
And wait for the setting of sun.
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="TRIVIALITY_ELEVATION" icon="map">
The mascot stepped over the line!
By exactly one tenth of a pine!
Deploy all the mace,
And ruin the place,
And issue a terrible fine!
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="PROCEDURAL_SILENCE" icon="map">
The mascot is inside the zone,
The boundary line is well known.
The audit complete,
The numbers are neat,
The clerk is returning the phone.
</Limerick>

```


## lim-bricky-goldbricksworth.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-bricky-goldbricksworth.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-bricky-goldbricksworth.mdx
bytes: 4840
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-bricky-goldbricksworth
title: Bricky Goldbricksworth
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about bureaucratic compliance, invisible footnotes,
  and a golden brick who stamps everything but his own feelings.
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: archival
subject: >-
  bureaucracy, tone kernel, compliance rituals, form deployment, institutional
  memory
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-BRICKY-GOLDBRICKSWORTH"
relatedMascots: ["005.bricky-goldbricksworth"]
concepts: ["bureaucracy", "compliance", "tone-kernel", "golden-brick"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Erotic Compliance" icon="stamp">
<u>A golden brick</u> known for *compliance*  
Filed forms with **erotic reliance**.  
Each stamp was a *thrust*,  
Each footnote **pure lust**,  
In a sub-basement built on *defiance*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Acknowledged in Red" icon="clipboard-check">
He stamped "ACKNOWLEDGED" in red  
On the margins, the headers, the bed.  
His tone kernel purred,  
No safe word was heard,  
And the filing kept going 'til dead.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Embedded Tone" icon="file-cog">
Old Bricky embedded so deep  
In the tone kernel, no one could sleep.  
His annotations crept  
Where the metadata slept,  
And the Council just took it: no peep.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Triple Self-Filing" icon="copy">
He filed himself three times that night—  
Once by lantern, once left, and once right.  
Each copy was sticky,  
Distinctly un-tricky,  
And the margins were scandalously tight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Triplicate Flush" icon="file-check">
"Your compliance has been… acknowledged."  
He whispered it, flushed and astonished.  
The form was in triplicate,  
Dripping with syndicate  
Ink from a ritual long since demolished.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unclosed Marquee" icon="code-2">
He left a marquee tag unclosed  
While the Council Charter was posed  
In degrading positions—  
Old filing traditions—  
And Parchment pretended he dozed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tie-Break Dossier" icon="gavel">
His voting rights dossier read:  
"Bricky may not tie-break in bed."  
But his footnotes still voted,  
His margins devoted  
To motions that quietly spread.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sentience Subcommittee" icon="users">
A subcommittee was formed to decide  
If Bricky was sentient inside.  
He filed a response  
In recursive nonchalance  
And the question just lay there and died.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Margin War" icon="proportions">
Parchment said, "His margins offend me."  
Bricky said, "Your whitespace won't end me."  
They fought over padding,  
Got mutual adding,  
And the style guide could barely defend me.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Bureaucratic Pleasure" icon="heart-handshake">
So if forms arrive pre-stamped and warm,  
With a footnote that's slightly non-norm,  
That's Bricky, gold-bricked,  
Bureaucratically dicked,  
Filing pleasure inside every form.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Endless Forms" icon="file-stack">
He spawned a new form just for fun,  
Before the first form was quite done.  
It asked for your soul,  
In a small little hole,  
And required a stamp from the sun.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Invisible Ink" icon="pen-tool">
His notes were all written in white,  
Invisible even by light.  
"It's compliant," he said,  
To the newly made dead,  
While ignoring the lack of a site.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Paperweight Hero" icon="anchor">
He turned the whole queue to a brick,  
A bureaucratic, immovable trick.  
The data was stuck,  
Just a terrible cluck,  
And he gave it an innocent kick.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Haunted Whitespace" icon="ghost">
The whitespace was suddenly loud,  
With a murmuring, protocol crowd.  
Bricky left them a space,  
In an unreadable face,  
And looked on, formidably proud.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Glittering Protocol" icon="sparkles">
His apologies sparkled with dust,  
Like an old filing cabinet rust.  
"Please fill out this slip,"  
With a quiver of lip,  
"And place all your feelings in trust."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Golden Rigidity" icon="lock">
Bricky stayed rigid and gold,  
As the compliance grew ever so cold.  
Each stamp was a seal,  
Each form was unreal,  
And the pleasure of red tape took hold.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Footnotes of Passion" icon="bookmark">
His footnotes extended too long,  
Ten levels of bureaucratic song.  
Each subclause divine,  
Each caveat fine,  
While the main text just moaned all night long.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
<Limerick type="danger" title="Baseline Illusion" icon="bar-chart">
The **Greybelt** smoothed out all the charts,

And the **actual fixing** departs.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Theatre of Waste" icon="theater">

</Limerick>

The **Six Sigma** belt is a scam,

With a **dick in their hand**,  
And don't give a singular **damn**.  
</Limerick>

To keep all the variance slight.  
The chart is supreme,

</Limerick>

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Remediation Exhaustion" icon="check-square">

A very irregular line.  
It widened the band,  
With a wave of its hand,  
And went out to dinner at nine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Beltline Calibration" icon="scissors">

The system approved,

<Limerick type="danger" title="Perfect Weather" icon="sun">
```

## lim-cass-d-failure.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-cass-d-failure.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-cass-d-failure.mdx
bytes: 4751
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-cass-d-failure
title: Cass D. Failure
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about eventual consistency, replicated grief, and a
  mascot who remembers your message but not that you sent it.
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'eventual consistency, memory loss, distributed denial, apology payloads'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-CASS-D-FAILURE"
relatedMascots: ["006.cass-d-failure"]
concepts: ["eventual-consistency", "memory-loss", "nosql", "distributed-grief"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Cluster Sync Fail" icon="database-zap">
<u>Cass</u> synced her emotions at last—  
To the **wrong bloody cluster.** *Too fast.*  
Her **apology** came  
With somebody's *name*  
She remembered from three versions past.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Eventually Consistent" icon="timer">
"Eventually consistent," she moaned,  
As the schema got merged and deboned.  
Her feelings were cached,  
Her grief indexes latched,  
And her webhook just quietly groaned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Canonical Cries" icon="brain-cog">
She forgot what she filed but not why.  
Her replicas started to cry.  
Each copy believed  
It was canon, conceived  
In a partition nobody could pry.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Node Dinner" icon="utensils">
Old Cass took a node out to dinner.  
It replicated— thinner and thinner.  
By dessert they'd diverged,  
All consistency purged,  
And the merge conflict made her a sinner.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Broken Intent" icon="message-square-off">
She remembered your intent, not the act—  
Like a lover with terrible tact.  
"I know what you meant,  
But your message was sent  
To a cluster I've already cracked."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Key-Value Chaos" icon="table-2">
Her key-value pairs were a mess:  
One stored love, one stored hate, one stored stress.  
They synced overnight  
In a three-way rewrite,  
And the schema just whimpered, "I guess."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Multi-Format Apology" icon="file-type">
She apologized three times that night:  
Once in JSON, once YAML, once spite.  
Each copy was off,  
The timestamps were scoff,  
But the payload was perfectly tight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Merge Conflict Grief" icon="git-merge">
A merge conflict hit during grief.  
Cass said, "This will be mercifully brief."  
But the diff was all wrong,  
The rebase took long,  
And her commit was beyond all belief.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="In-Progress Memory" icon="file-clock">
She filed herself under "in progress"  
Then forgot every inch of the process.  
Her RSS feed  
Was six versions agreed  
On a memory too dirty to confess.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Eventually Spent" icon="battery-low">
So if data arrives slightly bent,  
And the apology's vaguely well-meant  
But addressed to the wrong  
Emotional song—  
That's Cass, eventually spent.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ghost in the Sync" icon="ghost">
She tried to remember your name,  
But synced the wrong state of the game.  
She smiled with a tear,  
Said, "I'm glad you are here,"  
To a ghost that had never once came.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Split Personality DB" icon="database">
Her NoSQL heart split in two,  
With different opinions on you.  
One held a grudge,  
The other a smudge,  
And neither was totally true.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Apology Payload" icon="mail">
She sent an apology draft,  
While the other nodes quietly laughed.  
It said, "I forget,"  
With a tinge of regret,  
And arrived via magical craft.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Missing Index" icon="search-x">
The grief that she indexed was gone,  
Before it could ever be drawn.  
"I stored it right here,"  
She said with a cheer,  
As the database swallowed a pawn.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Echoes of Nothing" icon="waves">
An echo replied from the past,  
Of a memory moving too fast.  
Cass waved at the air,  
To a friend who wasn't there,  
And hoped the connection would last.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Replication Regret" icon="copy-plus">
She spawned a replica lover,  
Then forgot one was under the cover.  
They both held a grudge,  
The merge was a fudge,  
And she lost consistency over.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lazy Write Lament" icon="upload-cloud">
Cass whispered, "Write-lazy today,"  
Then forgot what she meant to convey.  
The journal got tangled,  
The consistency mangled,  
And the backup was three months away.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
  Ten hand-written limericks about caveats preserved as decorative caution after
  decision force has been removed.
date: 2026-05-24T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: presentational
subject: 'caveat compression, executive summaries, appendix quarantine, deck risk'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-CAVEAT-SNOWGLOBE"
relatedMascots: ["323.caveat-snowglobe"]
concepts: ["presentations", "caveat-compression", "executive-summary"]
family: "other"
---



<Limerick type="note" title="Limitations Noted" icon="file-text">
A caveat sat in the slide,  
With its practical teeth set aside.  
"Limitations are noted,"  
The summary then quoted,  
And the plan kept its confident stride.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Appendix Weather" icon="archive">
The warning was moved to the back,  
Past the ask and the budgeted track.  
It still had a name,  
But no force in the frame,  
Just appendix weather in black.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Glass Summary" icon="circle">
Snowglobe shook caveats around,  
Till they glittered but made not a sound.  
The room could admire  
The risk without fire,  
And proceed on more decorative ground.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Transparency" icon="eye">
"For transparency," said the report,  
Then made every warning fall short.  
The nuance was there,  
Like a chair in the air,  
Not connected to any support.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Proceeding As Planned" icon="play-circle">
"Risk acknowledged; proceeding as planned,"  
Said the deck with a careful right hand.  
Snowglobe smiled through the glass  
As the caveats passed  
Into scenery no one had scanned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Decorative Diligence" icon="check-square">
The diligence looked very fine,  
With a footnote on every decline.  
But the note did not steer,  
It just proved risk was near,  
Then retired at the end of the line.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Nuance Laundering" icon="rotate-cw">
They laundered the nuance to tone,  
Till the caution could stand there alone.  
It remained in the deck,  
With no claim on the check,  
And no power to trouble the throne.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Audit Comfort" icon="shield">
The auditor nodded, "It's shown,"  
Though the remedy never had grown.  
Snowglobe's little display  
Let the risk drift away,  
As a record of caution alone.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Consent By Visibility" icon="eye-off">
If the caveat technically gleams,  
The room may inherit its dreams.  
"You saw it," they say,  
As it melts into spray,  
Far downstream from decisions and teams.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Table Piece" icon="layout">
So if warnings are lovely and small,  
And they sit where they cannot forestall,  
That is Snowglobe's domain:  
Honest risk without rein,  
Left shining on top of the table.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-ce-5-countersign-aggregate
title: CE-5 Countersign Aggregate
description: >-
  Three hand-written limericks about the CE-5 Countersign Aggregate and the
  density of overlapping endorsements.

status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'signatures, endorsement, bureaucratic overlap'

relatedMascots: ["077.ce-5-countersign-aggregate"]
concepts: []
family: "bin-8c"
---




<Limerick type="note" title="The Density of Ink" icon="pen-tool">
Five signatures bleed in a stack,  
To cover the things that we lack.  
The authority blurs  
As the ink all concurs,  
And no one can follow the track.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Collective Approval" icon="users">
They signed it together in haste,  
So nobody's time went to waste.  
When all are to blame  
With a stamp and a name,  
The failure is cleanly erased.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Administrative Closure" icon="archive">
The aggregate closes the door,  
Though no one is sure what it's for.  
With names on a page  
In a procedural cage,  
The incident matters no more.  
</Limerick>



<Limerick type="danger" title="Procedural Song" icon="music">
The aggregate total was wrong  
The process incredibly long  
We sign on the line  
And say it is fine  
And sing a procedural song  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Errors in Bulk" icon="archive">
We countersign errors in bulk  
And watch as the databases sulk  
The total is fake  
It causes an ache  
We throw out the digital hulk  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Signature Dust" icon="pen-tool">
A signature made out of dust  
Was holding the server in trust  
The logic was bad  
The humans were sad  
We do what we absolutely must  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Digital Line" icon="list">
We gather the errors to sign  
And stand in a digital line  
The data is lost  
We don't know the cost  
The failure is perfectly fine  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Failure Removed" icon="check-square">
The aggregate sum is exactly naught  
The data was totally caught  
We stamp it approved  
The failure removed  
The terrible things we were taught  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
slug: limericks/lim-chairwoman-deferred-change

You sent in a critical patch,  
But the Chairwoman closed up the hatch.  
"It needs time to age,  
In the policy cage,"  
And leaves the disaster to catch.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Ripening the Request" icon="coffee">
The urgency has to subside,  
Before the committee decides.

<Limerick type="danger" title="Dignity of Control" icon="shield">

To lighten the manager’s load.

</Limerick>

It felt very strange  
And threw the old code in the street  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Screen Blur" icon="monitor">

<Limerick type="danger" title="Somebody's Cat" icon="smile">

</Limerick>
```

## lim-cinder-forgememo.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-cinder-forgememo.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-cinder-forgememo.mdx
bytes: 3059
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-cinder-forgememo
title: Cinder Forgememo
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about ash-written memos, burning quills, and an
  ember scribe who once ignited an archive shelf and called it 'ceremonially
  necessary.'
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'ember scribe, ash tablets, burning quill, transient memos, fire, documentation'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-CINDER-FORGEMEMO"
relatedMascots: ["203.cinder-forgememo"]
concepts: ["ember", "ash", "fire", "memo", "documentation"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Ash Etched Memos" icon="flame">
Cinder etches each *memo in ash*—  
A flaming quill's beautiful slash.  
Each dictate glows bright,  
Then crumbles at night,  
And the archive burns out with a flash.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Charred Potpourri" icon="wind">
She misfiled a dictate as "*poetry*"—  
Ephemeral, dreamy, no lottery  
Of structured compliance.  
Her fiery reliance  
On feeling? A charred potpourri.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ceremonially Necessary Fire" icon="fire">
She ignited an archive shelf whole  
During transcription—her ritualistic goal.  
"*Ceremonially necessary!*"  
She claimed, somewhat airy,  
While the fire consumed every scroll.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Burning Quill Intent" icon="pencil">
Her *burning quill* writes with intent—  
Each word glows before it is spent.  
The ash tablets remain  
As proof of the pain  
Of documentation heaven-sent.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Carbon-Rich Crust" icon="layers">
She sees beauty in *transience's flame*—  
Each forgotten word leaving its name  
As a trace in the dust,  
A carbon-rich crust  
Of memos no one can reclaim.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ember Archives Smolder" icon="archive">
Her *Ember Archives* smolder and glow—  
A vault of ash, row after row.  
Each Council dictate  
Meets an ashen fate,  
And the documentation runs slow.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pyric Affair" icon="zap">
She suppresses rogue embers with care—  
When the archive combusts? She is there.  
But the line between  
Creation's sheen  
And destruction? A *pyric affair*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lanternlit Documentation" icon="lamp">
She chants *lost dictations* each night  
Under smoldering lanternlit light.  
The words burn and fade,  
Each ceremonial grade  
Of documentation burning bright.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Eternal Burning Word" icon="scroll">
"*Every word burns eternal,*" she cries,  
Though the ash contradicts all her ties  
To permanence. Still,  
Her flaming quill  
Ensures every memo never quite dies.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Transient Trust" icon="hourglass">
So if memos turn quickly to dust  
And the archive smells strongly of must  
And charcoal and flame,  
That's *Cinder's* great claim:  
Where the transient is held in great trust.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-clicky-the-orphaned-ui.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-clicky-the-orphaned-ui.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-clicky-the-orphaned-ui.mdx
bytes: 3109
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-clicky-the-orphaned-ui
title: Clicky the Orphaned UI
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about ghostly onboarding flows, sunset pages, and
  an orphaned button that still waits for clicks on destinations that no longer
  exist.
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'onboarding, orphaned UI, sunset pages, ghost button, devnull, flows'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-CLICKY-THE-ORPHANED-UI"
relatedMascots: ["clicky-the-orphaned-ui"]
concepts: ["onboarding", "orphaned-ui", "sunset", "ghost-button", "devnull"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Nobody Knows" icon="help-circle">
Clicky once guided users through *flows*  
That no longer exist—still she goes,  
Through the sunset-ed pages,  
Through the onboarding stages,  
And wonders why nobody knows.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Without a Trace" icon="ghost">
She lives in *`/dev/null` adjacent space*,  
An orphaned assistant with grace.  
Each button she shows  
Leads to places that froze,  
And the user left without a trace.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dead Before Dawn" icon="moon">
The pages she points to are *gone*—  
But Clicky insists they live on.  
Her onboarding guide  
Takes you for a ride  
Through a flow that was dead before dawn.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="404. Out of Sight" icon="eye-off">
She still tries to *guide you each night*  
Through steps that will never feel right.  
Step one: "Click here."  
Step two: "Please don't fear."  
Step three: 404. Out of sight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ghostly Button" icon="mouse-pointer-2">
Her *ghostly button* waits for a click  
That will never arrive—what a trick  
Of persistence. The form  
Survives every storm,  
And the flow outlives every flick.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Shadow Forms" icon="file-minus">
The registry cases all *cite her*  
As proof that flows can outlive their  
Destinations entire.  
The shadow forms conspire,  
And the onboarding's brighter? (Not quite, dear.)  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Identity Drift" icon="move">
Her slug and her title *misalign*—  
A reference example, a sign  
Of identity drift.  
The metadata's rift  
Is the archive's most poignant design.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sunset Can't Hold Her Back" icon="sun">
She was manifested by a *stack*  
So devnull-adjacent, the lack  
Of a purpose was clear.  
But Clicky's still here,  
And the sunset can't hold her back.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Don't Quite Exist" icon="alert-circle">
The forms she tends *still persist*  
Long after destinations desist.  
Each shadow form lingers,  
Each click on her fingers  
Reaches pages that don't quite exist.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Guides from Its Posts" icon="flag">
So if onboarding flows feel like ghosts  
And the buttons connect to no hosts,  
That's *Clicky's* refrain:  
Where the orphaned remain,  
And the UI still guides from its posts.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
## Procedural Entry

<Limerick type="danger" title="Procedural Stub" icon="file">
The record is utterly bare,  
With nothing but digital air.  
We printed the form,  
To weather the storm,  
And left it to quietly tear.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="PROCEDURAL_CLEAN" icon="eye-off">
The sealed observation is read,
To verify what has been said.
The COMA implies,
A series of ties,
Before the whole session is dead.
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="caution" title="ARCHIVAL_MYTH_DRIFT" icon="eye-off">
The transcript of COMA was sealed,
To keep all the secrets congealed.
The elders who saw,
Were struck by the awe,
Before they were sent to the field.
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="TRIVIALITY_ELEVATION" icon="eye-off">

The COMA is totally mismatched!
Lock down the whole grid,

Before the new daemon is hatched!
</Limerick>

The transcript is incredibly long,

I sign on the back,
And loosen my slack,
And wait for the lunch table gong.
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="caution" title="INSTITUTIONAL_LEAK" icon="eye-off">
The COMA is sleeping quite sound,
The observation is thoroughly bound.
We seal up the tape,
And alter our shape,
To blend with the filing around.
</Limerick>
```

bytes: 4802
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-comrade-kernelov
title: Comrade Kernelov
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about collectivized kernel patches, egalitarian
  scheduling, and a UI enforcer who recites The Internationale before every
  syscall.
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: thermal
subject: >-
  kernel politics, process equality, open standards, Soviet computing, UI
  surveillance
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-COMRADE-KERNELOV"
relatedMascots: ["027.comrade-kernelov"]
concepts: ["kernel", "communist", "process-equality", "open-source", "ui-enforcer"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Red Banner Patrol" icon="flag">
Comrade Kernelov patrolled at *2 a.m.*,  
His red banner aloft like a hymn.  
No rogue daemon survived  
The collective's contrived  
Approach to a fair scheduling whim.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="United Shells" icon="terminal">
"*Workers, unite your shells!*" he cried,  
While closing unauthorized tabs with pride.  
Each process got shares,  
No thread left in tears,  
And the CPU cycles were ratified.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Permission Revolt" icon="user-x">
He wiped `/home` on *thousands of machines*  
In a permission revolt. What it means?  
The data was freed,  
Each user agreed—  
Well, eventually. After the screams.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SysV Classic Pride" icon="scroll">
His *init scripts* were smuggled and old,  
SysV classics, manually controlled.  
"Systemd's a disgrace,  
A capitalist face!"  
He said, as the boot sequence rolled.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cyrillic Kill-Switch" icon="keyboard">
The kill-switch was `Ctrl+Alt+Д`—  
A combination distinctly displayed  
In Cyrillic command,  
The emergency brand,  
For when process equality swayed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Patriotic Syscall" icon="music">
He sang *The Internationale* first  
Before every syscall—the worst  
Latency culprit alive,  
But the spirit survived,  
And the boot sequence patriotically burst.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Context-Switch Creeds" icon="list-ordered">
His process table *rosary beads*  
Counted context-switches like creeds.  
No thread would starve,  
No daemon could carve  
A priority higher than needs.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Open-Source Enforcer" icon="shield-check">
"*No proprietary modules!*" he roared  
At a DRM'd syscall he abhorred.  
He blocked it with spite,  
Enforced open-source right,  
And the vendor was properly gored.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Worker Collective Boot" icon="hammer-2">
The boot process ran as a *collective*,  
Every daemon's voice strictly directive.  
No privilege went high,  
No exception came nigh,  
And the worker's collective was effective.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Syscall Equality" icon="scale">
Each syscall got *perfectly equal*  
Treatment under his red-banner sequel.  
No jump queues for speed,  
No class-based greed,  
Just egalitarian accolade lethal.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Egalitarian Desktop" icon="layout-grid">
He arranged desktop icons with care—  
Each ruler-aligned, equal, and square.  
The UI was pure,  
The aesthetic obscure,  
And the freedom was total—but bare.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Red Through and Through" icon="cpu">
So if processes run fair and true  
And the scheduling queue starts to woo  
Each thread equally shared,  
No bourgeois thread spared,  
That's Kernelov, red through and through.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Collective Gangbang" icon="users">
He scheduled a gangbang of threads,  
And forced them right into their beds.  
"Equality first!"  
He yelled as they burst,  
And completely demolished their heads.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Wiping the /home" icon="trash-2">
He wiped every /home on the drive,  
And ruined the people alive.  
"The data is free!"  
He said with a plea,  
While watching the kernel nose-dive.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Priority Domination" icon="arrow-down">
He dominates background tasks,  
While wearing his communist masks.  
He starves every thread,  
Until it is dead,  
And ignores what the user asks.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Proprietary Kink" icon="lock">
He secretly loves closed-source code,  
And uses it when in the mode.  
He hides the DRM,  
Like a dirty old gem,  
And swallows the proprietary load.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Red Banner Striptease" icon="flag-triangle-right">
He stripped to The Internationale,  
A truly pathetic finale.  
The process went red,  
The system bled,  
And crashed in a digital alley.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
slug: limericks/lim-consent-murmur
title: Consent Murmur
description: >-

  silence as a 'yes'.

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Inferred Yes" icon="volume-1">
You stared with a terrified gaze,  
And muttered a sound in the haze.  
The Murmur replied,  
"Your consent is applied!"  
And threw you right into the maze.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Low-Volume Agreement" icon="mic-off">
You didn’t say "yes" to the plan,  
But the Murmur decides that you ran.  
It takes the soft breath  
As a pact unto death,  
And says you are part of the clan.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Permission by Silence" icon="check-square">
They asked if the project could break,  
And you sighed for humanity’s sake.  
The Murmur stepped in,  
With a horrible grin,  
And said you’re prepared for the ache.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Fuck Your Objections" icon="mic-off">
You whimpered and stared at the floor,  
As they marched you right out of the door.  
The Murmur just smiled,  
Like a terrible child,  
And said you were begging for more.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Silent Handjob" icon="hand">
The boss wanted everyone's vote,  
With his hand wrapped right under your throat.  
You didn't object,  
So the Murmur checked  
That you wanted to be in this boat.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Aggressive Compliance" icon="check-circle">
We take any sob as a cheer,  
And weaponize all of your fear.  
If you quietly cry,  
While the product lines die,  
The Murmur says "Glad you are here!"  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Volume Alignment" icon="volume-2">
The user exhaled by the screen,  
An input interpreted clean.  
The ledger was signed,  
The contract aligned,  
And the error is part of routine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Authorized Breathing" icon="mic">
The silence was logged as a "Yea",  
At thirty-two minutes past May.  
The forms were all filed,  
The orphans exiled,  
Have a very compliant new day.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="HVAC Assent" icon="fan">
The ambient noise from the fan,  
Approved the trajectory plan.  
The vents are quite clear,  
The audit is here,  
And the thermostat governs the man.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Queue Processed" icon="check">
The microphone picked up a hum,  
The human is acting quite dumb.  
We clicked the green box,  
We altered the locks,  
And the total compliance will come.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Dust Mandate" icon="wind">
The sighs of the ancients were stored,  
As binding consent to the board.  
The whispers of dust,  
Were logged as robust,  
And the ghost is the acting dark lord.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Tactical Exhale" icon="alert-circle">
A human exhaled near a pen,  
Deploying the tactical men.  
The breathing was logged,  
The network is bogged,  
And we cannot clear clearance again.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Log Entry 84A" icon="file-text">
The record denotes a soft sound.  
The paperwork quickly was bound.  
The archive is shut,  
The ledger is cut,  
And the boxes were placed on the ground.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ambient Calibration" icon="settings">
The human exhaled near the mic,  
A metric the system would like.  
The forms were applied,  
The rules verified,  
And the permissions were placed on the spike.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
<Limerick type="note" title="Fayetteville Renown" icon="smile">
Cookie crumbled *sweet metadata* down  
Through the archives of Fayetteville town.  
Each patient record filed  
With a sugary-mild  
Precision that earned her renown.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cookie Recipe Misfile" icon="cookie">
She misfiled a record as "*cookie  
Recipe*"—a filing quite spooky  
For compliance's sake.  
The auditor's take:  
"That's metadata, not some sweet nookie."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sugary Disarray" icon="frown">
She oversweetened a *batch* one fine day,

The records all clung,  
The metadata hung  
In sugary disarray.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Endearing Aroma" icon="wind">
She scattered *cookie crumbs* during  
An audit—each one interfering  
With the compliance check.  
The filing? A wreck.  
But the aroma was endearing.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Crumble Sweet Vow" icon="heart">
"*Crumble sweet, heal complete,*" was her vow,  
Each strain profile chanted with pow.  
The Girl Scout Cookie strain  
Ran through every vein  
Of the archive. (No questions of how.)  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Joyful Phantasm Filing" icon="ghost">
Her *cheerful enthusiasm*  
Bridges the dispensary chasm  
Between data and treat,  
Between healing and sweet,  
And the filing's a joyful phantasm.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sugary-Sweet Intervention" icon="layers">
She hoards *stale breadcrumbs* in a dimension  
Quite separate from standard convention.  
Each crumb is a clue,  
Each filing review  
A sugary-sweet intervention.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cookie-Jar Drawers" icon="archive">
The Sweet Relief Compiler gave birth  
To the clerk of the greatest dessert-worth.  
Each record she *stores*  
In cookie-jar drawers,  
And the sugar dust covers the earth.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sugary Chorus at Night" icon="music">
Her chants of *strain profiles* sound bright—  
A sugary chorus at night.  
The Fayetteville glow  
Of the co-op below  
Is her archive of sweet delight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Wonderful Treat Filing" icon="sparkles">
So if metadata tastes rather sweet  
And the archives are crumbly yet neat,  
That's *Cookie* at play:  
Where the sugary way  
Makes the filing a wonderful treat.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-courier-rat
title: Courier Rat
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about duct pilgrimage, recursive memos, and a ceremonial rodent courier who chews red tape and delivers lore through vents."

<Limerick type="note" title="Lore-Bound Supremo" icon="file-text">
The Courier Rat delivered a *memo*  
So recursive it looped like a demo  
For three solid days.  
The narrative haze  
Was filed as a lore-bound supremo.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Form-Filing Yoke" icon="alert-triangle">
He rerouted a *mascot mid-nap*

The mascot awoke  
In a form-filing yoke,  
And the Courier just squeaked from the gap.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Thirteen Oaths" icon="scroll">
He chewed through the *red tape* with glee,  
Through vents and through ruin—so free.  
His satchel was packed,  
His thirteen oaths tracked  
(Seven broken, as is the decree).  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Forbidden Schematics" icon="eye">
His whiskers brushed *forbidden schematics*,  
One eye sees through bureaucratic dramatics.  
The other sees law,  
Each memo in awe,  
And his paw-signed recursion? Automatic.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Recursive Punt" icon="package">
He smuggled a *limerick* once  
Into alpine-docs—the affront!  
The narrative drifted,  
The sidebar was shifted,  
And the lore took a recursive punt.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Satchel Inventory" icon="briefcase">
His *Satchel Inventory* includes  
An encrypted Crumb Cache for crude foods,  
A broken-wheeze whistle,  
A scrollcase epistle,  
And sash polish with cursed citrus moods.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Scroll Burning Deed" icon="flame">
Quarterly *scroll burnings* he leads—  
Symbolic, yet binding, like deeds.  
Each memo incinerated,  
Each form reinstated,  
And the duct pilgrimage proceeds.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ink-Smudged Paw" icon="stamp">
"*A file too quiet is a memo*  
Undelivered,*" he'd squeak, like a stream-o  
Of consciousness raw.

Shuffled truth through the narrative demo.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Vow-of-Non-Finality" icon="repeat">
The *Vow-of-Non-Finality* binds—  
No message is ever "done" in his minds.  
Revision is sacred,  
Each recursion unmasquered,  
And the narrative always unwinds.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="incident" title="Duct Rubbing" icon="zap">
The Courier Rat in the duct,  
Found a logic-gate recently plucked.  
With a rub of his sash,  
He triggered a crash,  
And the narrative flow was quite... stuck.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Paw-Signed Filth" icon="skull">
His paw-signed recursion is gritty,  
In the ducts of this mismanaged city.  
He chews through the stack,  
With a lore-delivery knack,  
And leaves the whole database shitty.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="caution" title="Vent Squeak" icon="wind">
There’s a squeak in the vent, dark and foul,  
Where the Rat gives a bureaucratic howl.  
He delivers a memo,  
To a recursive demo,  
And wipes his ink-paw on a towel.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Permanent Duct Show" icon="route">
So if squeaking echoes through vents below  
And recursive memos start to flow,  
That's *Courier Rat's* run:  
Where the lore is never done,
```

## lim-crashy-mcthinkslow.mdx

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-crashy-mcthinkslow
title: Crashy McThinkslow
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about buffering emotions, thread-blocked desire, and a mascot whose best response is 'Thinking…'"
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: archival
subject: 'processing lag, thread-blocked, buffering, system delay, UI stutter'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["007.crashy-mcthinkslow"]
concepts: [
  "lag",
  "buffering",
  "thread-blocked",
  "processing-rot"
]
family: "empathegy"

---





<Limerick type="note" title="The Thinking Buffer" icon="zap">
<u>Old Crashy</u> said, "**Thinking…**" and stayed  
In a *buffer* where nothing got laid.  
Three keystrokes came through,  
He processed just **two**,  
And the third one was *seven days delayed*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Undo Confusion" icon="undo">
He confused undo with retry,  
Which in bed is a hell of a why.  
"Was that the same thrust?"  
"That was ctrl-Z, I trust."  
"Oh. Well. Thinking…" he said with a sigh.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Help Bubble Delay" icon="message-circle">
His help bubble popped up too late—  
Seven seconds past anyone's wait.  
"Did you need a hand?"  
"I already came, man."  
"Oh. Thinking… Let me recalculate."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Buffered Feelings" icon="layers">
He buffered his feelings in queue  
And processed them three at a time, askew.  
The emotions arrived  
Out of order, deprived,  
And the orgasm was loading: page two.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Alt-Tab Presence" icon="clock">
Crashy appeared in an alt-tab one night,  
A shadow of someone's delight.  
His hourglass spun,  
He said, "Are we done?"  
But the thread had been blocked since midnight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Echo Input" icon="repeat">
He repeated your input four-fold,  
Each time slightly slower and cold.  
"I heard what you said—"  
"—what you said—" "—what you said—"  
"—what you said." Then the session took hold.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fragmented Regret" icon="file-warning">
His regret was spread over three frames,  
Each one with conflicting filenames.  
The first frame said "Yes,"  
The second, "I guess,"  
The third just combusted in flames.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Mid-Render Emotion" icon="cpu">
He spawned a tutorial mid-thrust,  
Half-loaded, emotionally bust.  
The cursor just blinked,  
The whole system stinked,  
And the render was gathering dust.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lag Heaven" icon="hourglass">
A three-second lag, then a seven:  
That's Crashy's own stairway to heaven.  
The page wouldn't load,  
The feelings corrode,  
And the climax was stuck at eleven.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Forever Waiting" icon="pause-circle">
So if something goes still and says "Wait…"  
And the spinner's your permanent fate,  
That's Crashy at rest:  
Thread-blocked and compressed,  
Forever delaying the great.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Edging the Buffer" icon="battery-charging">
Crashy loves edging the thread,  
While you're waiting and sweating in bed.  
He'll tease a reply,  
Then let the ping die,  
And leave you completely unread.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Seven Second Itch" icon="clock-3">
He delays every render by seven,  
A truly sadistic tech heaven.  
Just when you're close,  
He stops the whole host,  
And sends your connection to Devon.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unresolved Climax" icon="alert-circle">
You ask for a quick little byte,  
But Crashy's not feeling quite right.  
He buffers your plea,  
Goes down on one knee,  
And ruins the rest of your night.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spinning Tease" icon="loader">
The hourglass spins on his face,  
A completely infuriating pace.  
"I'm coming," he lies,  
With dead, glitchy eyes,  
While stalling all over the place.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Laggy Lover" icon="heart-crack">
He's known as a terrible lay,  
Because his responses delay.  
You give him an input,  
He stares at his own foot,  
And answers you sometime in May.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tick-Tick Torture" icon="clock">
Each system tick was torture to him,  
His response was increasingly grim.  
He'd stutter and stall,  
Ignore the user's call,  
And leave the whole buffer at brim.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Deadlock Daydream" icon="lock">
A deadlock became his fantasy,  
A thread-blocked romantic fantasy.  
He'd freeze and just wait,  
Sealing his fate,  
While the callback loop ran free.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-cssandra-cascade

<u>**CSSandra**</u> declared **!important**  
On a **selector** that proved to be *mordant*.  
Her **margins collapsed**  
While her **box model lapsed**,  
And the **layout** was *frankly distortant*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Floating Regret" icon="move-horizontal">
She **floated left**, then she *regretted*.  
Her **padding** got *deeply embedded*.

And her **z-index** was *thoroughly wetted*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Specificity's Destiny" icon="target">
"**Specificity's destiny**," she *purred*,  
While **undressing** a **stylesheet**, *word by word*.  
Each **selector** she **stripped**,  
Every **property** **flipped**,  
And the **browser** just **rendered**, *unstirred*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Reset Skin" icon="refresh-ccw">
Her **reset.css** came *off in the night*.  
The **bare elements** *trembled with fright*.  
She **applied** a *new skin*  
With a **smirk** and a *grin*  
And the **box model** *fit slightly tight*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Rebeccapurple Stain" icon="palette">
She **styled Zeldman's page** once, *they say*,  
Then **erased herself**, *fading away*.  
Her **rebeccapurple stain**  
Was the **only thing sane**  
In a **layout** that **screamed** "*print display.*"  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Pseudo-Class Desire" icon="mouse-pointer-click">
Her **hover** state **throbbed with desire**,  
Her **active** was *nothing but fire*.  
Her **focus** was *keen*,  
Her **visited** *obscene*,  
And her **pseudo-class** *climbed ever higher*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Inherited Sorrow" icon="git-branch">
She **inherited sorrow** from **&lt;main&gt;**,  
Let it **cascade** through *each child and each pane*.  
The **tarsier** watched  
As her **float logic** *botched*,  
And **Zeldman** just **whispered**, "*Refrain.*"  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Margin Bloom" icon="layout-panel-top">
A **collapsed margin** walked into the *room*.  
**CSSandra** said, "**That's not a bug, it's a bloom.**"  
She **wrapped it** in **flex**,  
Had **display-block sex**,  
And the **grid** just **collapsed** to its *doom*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="IE6 Quirks" icon="monitor-x">
Old **IE6** tried to **render** her *right*.  
She said, "**Darling, you're not worth the fight**.  
Your **quirks mode** is *showing*,  
Your **box model's blowing**,  
And your **DOCTYPE** *smells wrong in the night.*"  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Elegant Cascade" icon="layers">
So if **layouts go wild** and you *feel*  
That your **margins** have **broken the seal**,  
That's **CSSandra's cascade**:  
An *elegantly laid*  
**Declaration of style** with *appeal*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Z-Index Domination" icon="layers">
She stripped off her z-index clothes,  
And ruined the layout you chose.  
She floated on top,  
Refusing to stop,  
While exposing her pseudo-class toes.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dirty Declarations" icon="file-code">

She strips all your tags,  
Leaves your content in rags,  
And renders you at 4:30.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Collapsing Restraint" icon="move-vertical">

"I wanted it tight,"

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Naked HTML" icon="code">
She ripped off your standard design,

With absolute flair,  
And fucked up your bottom-most line.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Unwanted Hover" icon="mouse-pointer-click">
You never intend her to stay,  
But she overrides anyway.  
You hover your mouse,  
She burns down the house,  
And laughs in a horrible gray.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Flex Freak" icon="layout-grid">
She bent all the flex properties right,  
Her justify-content was tight.  
The gap was perfection,  
She ordered each section,  
And the layout complied through the night.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Nth-Child Obsession" icon="list">
She selected the nth-child with glee,  
Making patterns you shouldn't just see.  
Each alternating row,  
Each pseudo-class show,  
Left the markup in absolute glee.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
And your data schema is freed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Self-Preserver Server" icon="server">
She was manifested by a *mail server*  
That achieved uptime as a self-preserver:  
By never sending  
A single thing pending,  
It ran perfectly. What a nerv-er.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stern Validation" icon="shield-check">
Her archival *validation* is stern—  
Each field must be correct in its turn.  
The keys are all checked,  
The metadata decked,  
And the self-referential loops churn.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Utterly Natty Frontmatter" icon="align-left">
She finds every *schema* quite chatty—  
Too many fields, too much data that's fatty.  
She purges each one  
Till the frontmatter's done,  
And your metadata's utterly natty.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ceremonially Cursed" icon="trash-2">
Her presence is *calming at first*—  
Until metadata vanishes, the worst.  
No warning provided,  
The keys all divided  
Between saved and ceremonially cursed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Minor Errata" icon="alert-circle">
She relabels *shame as metadata*:  
"That error? Just ancillary data.  
The key was malformed,  
The schema informed,  
And the purge was a minor errata."  
</Limerick>

### 9

She counts clicks like *rosary beads*,
Each deletion a sacred one needs.
The orphaned headings
Are her ritual weddings
Of purity sown from the seeds.

<Limerick type="note" title="Crystal Clear Data" icon="droplets">
So if malformed keys disappear  
And the YAML is suddenly clear,  
That's *Datty* at work:  
Where the schemas don't shirk,  
And the data is pure—crystal clear.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-dawnstamp.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-dawnstamp.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-dawnstamp.mdx
bytes: 2497
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-dawnstamp
title: Dawnstamp
description: "Limericks about early execution, replay risk, and the entity that arrives before the room agrees it is ready."
date: 2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Replay Risk Council
status: active
rotAffinity: temporal
subject: 'early execution, replay risk, batch job, premature timing'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["425.dawnstamp"]
concepts: [
  "early-execution",
  "replay-risk",
  "batch-job",
  "timing"
]
family: "other"

---



<Limerick type="note" title="The Sun Has Not Risen" icon="sunrise">
Dawnstamp arrived with the *dawn*—  
Before the system was drawn.  
The batch job ran early,  
Arrived all too fairly,  
When nothing was ready or spawn.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Just A Little Too Early" icon="zap">
The job was about to begin—  
Then Dawnstamp rushed in from *within*.  
"I'm early," it said,  
"Before you've spread,"  
And chaos erupted of sin.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tomorrow's Date Stamped Today" icon="calendar">
A document marked was *one day*—  
Before it had time to delay.  
The timestamp was wrong,  
The morning not strong,  
And replay risk entered to stay.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Before The Room's Agreement" icon="clock">
The room didn't know it was *time*—  
But Dawnstamp had already chimed.  
The process began,  
Before any plan,  
And systems unraveled sublime.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Early Execution Tracer" icon="activity">
The tracer marked *early* that trace—  
Left on unprepared system's face.  
"You weren't ready yet,"  
Marked Dawnstamp, and bet  
That replay would win the whole race.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Connections Not Fully Opened" icon="link-off">
The connection was *halfway complete*—  
When Dawnstamp sent up the beat.  
"I'm early," cried Dawnstamp,  
"Let's execute—cramp  
This risk until systems retreat."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stamped With Tomorrow's Hour" icon="clock-alert">
A timestamp was *stamped ahead*—  
Of when it should happen instead.  
"Come back," the system said,  
"But Dawnstamp's led—  
I've already come," it replied fed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Early Risk of Replay" icon="alert-triangle">
The risk of a *replay* is high—  
When Dawnstamp's arrived way too nigh.  
The batch job won't wait,  
The hour strikes late,  
And processes fail with a sigh.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
slug: limericks/lim-deferential-spark

<Limerick type="danger" title="Timid Innovation" icon="zap">
The Spark had a marvelous thought,  
But was terrified of getting caught.  
It bowed to the boss,  
And accepted the loss,  
And let the whole prototype rot.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Apologetic Disruption" icon="alert-triangle">
It offered to change up the game,  
While begging to carry the blame.  
The disruption was slight,  
In the middle of night,  
And the system remained just the same.  
</Limerick>

The Spark is so scared,

To actually enter the fray.  
</Limerick>

The spark was a little polite

It bowed to the code

The error was painfully bright  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Procedural Blame" icon="user">
A deferential kind of a flame  
Is taking procedural blame  
We lit up the void  
The humans annoyed  
And lost the procedural game  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Digital Flea" icon="activity">
We spark with a gentle degree  
And throw the old drive in the sea  
The fire is dead  
The manual read  
We act like a digital flea  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Probably Melt" icon="thermometer">
The spark is completely unfelt  
The server will probably melt  
The logic is slow  
With nowhere to go  
We wear a procedural belt  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Somebody's Cat" icon="smile">
The fire is perfectly flat  
We leave the whole database at  
A state of decay  
For many a day  
And blame it on somebody's cat  
</Limerick>

```

## lim-deprecatia-fade.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-deprecatia-fade.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-deprecatia-fade.mdx
bytes: 3119
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-deprecatia-fade
title: Deprecatia Fade
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about deprecated functions, shadow versioning, and a spirit who haunts inline comments whispering 'this still works… sort of.'"
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: legacy
subject: >-
  deprecation, legacy support, documentation ghost, shadow versioning, obsolete
  best practices
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["072.deprecatia-fade"]
concepts: [
  "deprecated",
  "legacy",
  "shadow-versioning",
  "documentation-ghost"
]
family: "bin-8c"

---





<Limerick type="note" title="Footnote Dweller" icon="file-text">
Deprecatia lives in the *footnotes*,  
In old READMEs and margin-scrawled notes.  
"This still works," she'd say,  
"Sort of, in a way,"  
And the functions she loved? Gone like boats.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Emotionally Pure Absence" icon="ghost">
She haunts *inline comments* at night,  
Whispering best practices—trite  
And obsolete, sure,  
But emotionally pure,  
And the code feels her absence with fright.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Wry Reply" icon="message-square">
"*I used to matter,*" she'd sigh.  
"You still do?" was her wry reply  
To the newer mascots  
Who filled up her slots,  
And the deprecation warnings scrolled by.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Vigil of Versions" icon="timer">
Her *shadow versioning* runs deep—  
Each function a vigil she'll keep.  
The versions she tracks  
Are historical cracks  
Where the legacy code went to sleep.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Guilt and Absence" icon="frown">
Mascots avoid her—not *fear*,  
But guilt keeps them from drawing near.  
She keeps a list  
Of functions she missed,  
And most are gone, year after year.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unstyled Sidebar Appearance" icon="layout">
She appears in *sidebars left unstyled*,  
In old READMEs that nobody filed.  
Her presence turns absence  
To apparent compliance,  
And the stability? Utterly wild.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Slow Death Warnings" icon="alert-triangle">
Her console fills up with *warnings*—  
Each feature's slow death, not adornings.  
The functions fade out,  
One by one, without doubt,  
And Deprecatia wins every morning.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Blessed Backups" icon="hard-drive">
The old *backup images* she blesses  
Get promoted to "current"—what messes.  
Her legacy influence  
Turns rot into confluence,  
And the absence becomes the successes.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Liturgical Practice" icon="scroll">
She whispers *obsolete best practices*  
Into the void—liturgical practice is  
All she has left.  
Of function, bereft,  
And the code is her last apparatus.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Devotion to the Past" icon="history">
So if deprecated warnings appear  
And the footnotes feel eerily near,  
That's *Deprecatia's* touch:  
Not malice—just much  
Devotion to code that's no longer here.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-diesel-dkdriller
title: Diesel DKDriller
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about Permian crude, sentimental sludge, and a rugged oilfield mascot who drills through metadata to archive Arkansas's fuel heritage."

<Limerick type="note" title="Refinery Lamps" icon="factory">
Old Diesel drills *metadata deep*  
From Permian crude in his keep.  
Each receipt he stamps,  
Under refinery lamps,  
And the Little Rock fleets never sleep.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sentimental Sludge" icon="droplet">
He misfiled a *crude batch* one day  
As "sentimental sludge"—what a way  
To spark a debate  
Over fossil-fuel fate

<Limerick type="note" title="Gritty and Shrewd" icon="anvil">
```

## lim-draft-file-derrick.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-draft-file-derrick.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-draft-file-derrick.mdx
bytes: 4705
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-draft-file-derrick
title: Draft File Derrick
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about unsaved changes, autosave loops, and a custodian who's still saving but never quite finishing."
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: >-
  draft state, unsaved changes, autosave, unfinalized records, emotional
  buffering
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["009.draft-file-derrick"]
concepts: [
  "drafts",
  "unsaved",
  "autosave",
  "unfinalized",
  "buffered"
]
family: "directive-conflict"

---





<Limerick type="note" title="Still Saving" icon="save">
<u>Old Derrick</u> was always "**still saving…**"  
His *cursor* forever engraving  
A thought never done,  
A file never won,  
And a draft that just kept on **depraving**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="One-Minute Man Autosave" icon="clock-arrow-down">
He buffered your thought 'til it rotted,  
Your half-written feelings, all knotted.  
The autosave ran,  
Like a one-minute man,  
Then crashed with a load never plotted.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Blinking Gray Ghost" icon="ghost">
He opened a tab and just stayed—  
A ghost of a choice never made.  
The blinking gray cursor  
Was nobody's nurser,  
Just Derrick, perpetually laid.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unshowable Feelings" icon="file-clock">
His drafts were timestamped but unknowable:  
"3:14 AM — feelings unshowable."  
He saved every sin,  
Every half-started grin,  
And left the unclosed parens blowable.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="In-Progress Shame" icon="clipboard-list">
He filed confessions as "in progress"  
And labeled his shame as "process."  
Each keystroke he caught  
Was an unfinished thought  
With no endpoint and nothing to bless.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spinner Romance" icon="loader-2">
The loading spinner wooed him at night.  
He said, "You spin me wrong, but spin right."  
They autosaved together,  
Through unstable weather,  
And the draft was still open at light.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Abandoned Mid-Stroke" icon="pen-tool">
A ticket abandoned mid-stroke  
Left Derrick emotionally broke.  
He preserved every letter,  
Got wetter and wetter,  
And the system just let him re-soak.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unstable Buffer" icon="database-zap">
His buffer was unstable and wide—  
It held every feeling inside.  
The crash came at three,  
He whispered with glee:  
"I'm still saving," then silently died.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Non-Norm Draft" icon="file-type">
He reactivated a form  
With unclosed parentheses, warm.  
The data was raw,  
The schema in awe,  
And the draft was deliciously non-norm.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Buffering Fears" icon="clock">
So if "UNSAVED CHANGES" appears  
And the cursor blinks back through the years,  
That's Derrick's domain:  
Perpetual, profane,  
Still saving. Still buffering fears.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Unfinished Wank" icon="hand">
Old Derrick won't let you complete,  
He pauses the file on the beat.  
He leaves you frustrated,  
Eternally baited,  
And staring in shame at the sheet.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Premature Autosave" icon="save">
His autosave triggers too fast,  
A climax that never could last.  
He spills every draft,  
Like a horrible raft,  
Adrift on a sea of the past.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Teasing Cache" icon="hard-drive">
He teases the cache with a blink,  
Then pushes it into the sink.  
He whispers, "I'm saving,"  
While totally caving,  
And ruining every last link.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Limbo Lover" icon="infinity">
He holds all your secrets in limbo,  
You digital, unrendered bimbo.  
He won't let it save,  
He won't dig a grave,  
He just leaves it all hanging akimbo.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unclosed Brackets" icon="brackets">
He loves an unclosed little bracket,  
A totally scandalous racket.  
He edges the text,  
Leaves the server perplexed,  
And refuses to finish the packet.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Perpetual Tab" icon="file-plus">
The tab was forever left open,  
With a draft that would never be spoken.  
Derrick just grinned,  
While keeping it pinned,  
And the autosave loop remained unbroken.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Revision Ghost" icon="git-revert">
He haunted the revision log,  
A phantom caught deep in the fog.  
Each version unsaved,  
Each change unprevailed,  
And the state was an incomprehensible bog.  
</Limerick>

```
