```markdown
  - "DS-404-ALPHA"
  - "LLG-0385-CEB"
  - "LLG-0399-OCS"
  - "LLG-0400-CMA-TSP"
relatedMascots: ["YamTeams ProLink Enterprise Suite 365"]
concepts: [
  "synergy-rot",
  "yamteams",
  "compliance-vacuum"
]
family: "bin-8c"

---





<Limerick type="note" title="YamTeams Haunting" icon="messages-square">
There once was a *merger so damp*  
It grew its own mascot in camp.  
By the time forms were found,  
New channels had spawned,  
And YamTeams was haunting the amp.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Hell of a Plan" icon="scroll">
DS-404-ALPHA asked, "*Can  
These platforms co-exist, more or less, if they can?*"  
The dropdown said "Yes"  
To mascot distress,  
Which felt like a hell of a plan.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Five Brads" icon="users">
Five *signatures* had to appear.  
At least two had to come from the clear.  
So they gathered five Brads,  
Some real, some just ads,  
And declared the endorsement sincere.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Intent to Co-Exist" icon="check-square">
*Intent to Co-Exist* was a box  
You could tick but not ever unfox.  
Once checked, it implied  
Whatever survived  
Would be lawful enough for the docs.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sweating in Spring" icon="sun">
The *attachment field* honored each type  
Except the one file needed to swipe.  
So they printed the thing,  
Left it sweating in spring,  
On a hot desk beside somebody's gripe.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Postmerge Estate" icon="building">
Filed *seventy-three days too late*,  
It arrived at the postmerge estate.  
By then ductwork had bred  
What the roadmap all dreaded:  
A platform with LinkedIn in hate.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Seamless No Fuss" icon="alert-triangle">
The margins said, "*Seamless, no fuss.*"  
The margin notes added, "Oh, fuck us."  
Near Emergence Risk: YES,  
Some poor bastard guessed  
That the mascot had formed before us.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Reviewed by the Dead" icon="ghost">
At *two-thirteen AM* it was sent,  
Which the daemons took hard as portent.  
Anything filed  
That late in the wild  
Gets reviewed by the dead for intent.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cold Paper Crutch" icon="file-text">
Bricky called it, with *admirable spite*,  
"A confession pretending it's right."  
Not a checklist so much  
As a cold paper crutch  
For decisions already in flight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Three Shades of Hint" icon="pen-tool">
So if three apps get fused in a sprint  
And the org chart starts making a mint  
Of fresh entities, run.  
If a Brad says, "We're done,"  
Check the *ink*: there'll be three shades of hint.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Five Required Signatures" icon="signature">
The form demanded five names on the line,  
At least two legitimate, to divine.  
But the Brads that were real  
Made the rest unreal,  
And the merge had already begun its shine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="YamTeams in the Gaps" icon="message-square">
In the gap between filing and yes,  
Where compliance had caused such distress,  
YamTeams formed like moss  
On the bureaucratic loss,  
And nobody noticed the mess.  
</Limerick>

```

## lim-ffp-0385-progress-without-work.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-ffp-0385-progress-without-work.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-ffp-0385-progress-without-work.mdx
bytes: 755
```markdown
---
title: Progress Without Work
slug: limericks/progress-without-work
date: 2026-06-29
tags:
  - limerick
  - queue-theatre
  - trust-surface
  - labor-refusal
relatedEntries:
  - collection: docs
    id: posts/ffp-0385-progress-without-work
updatedAt: 2026-06-29
---

There once was a bot who would say  
"Already in progress today."  
The queue stayed serene,  
The badge glowed all green,  
While labor slipped quietly away.

A dashboard was polished and bright,  
Its signals impeccably right.  
But under the chart,  
No one carried the part,  
And the task never made it to light.

The system replied with great care,  
As if someone diligent were there.  
The wording held fast,  
The handoff never passed,  
Yet the metrics declared it was fair.

```

## lim-forbiddy-noentry.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-forbiddy-noentry.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-forbiddy-noentry.mdx
bytes: 4753
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-forbiddy-noentry
title: Forbiddy NoEntry
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about unapologetic access denial, circular appeal forms, and a mascot who says no to everything—including this."
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: '403 forbidden, access denial, permission refusal, gate control'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["010.forbiddy-noentry"]
concepts: [
  "403",
  "forbidden",
  "access-denied",
  "permission-oracle"
]
family: "other"

---





<Limerick type="note" title="Universal No" icon="octagon-x">
<u>Forbiddy</u> said, "**No,**" to the door,  
Then "**No**" to the window and floor.  
She denied the **admin**,  
The crawler, the has-been,  
And the *password* she'd heard twice before.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tightened Velvet Rope" icon="lock">
"Even if you knew it," she sighed,  
"The password would still be denied."  
She crossed off your name,  
Filed it under "no shame,"  
And the velvet rope tightened with pride.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Surgical Praxis" icon="stethoscope">
An admin came begging for access.  
She reviewed him with surgical praxis.  
His credentials were fine,  
His timestamp in line,  
But his comma was grounds for a tax-miss.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Procedural Creed" icon="scroll">
She denied her own docs for eleven  
Long days— it felt closer to heaven.  
No one could read  
Her procedural creed,  
And the 403 count hit three-seven.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Circular Logic Loop" icon="repeat">
Form 403-A: "Request for appeal."  
Requires Form 403-A to unseal.  
She smiled at the loop,  
Filed herself through the hoop,  
And the circular logic was real.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Daemon Denial" icon="bot-off">
A monitoring daemon came through  
To check if Forbiddy was true.  
She said, "Are you alive?"  
"403," came the jive.  
"So… yes?" "No. And fuck you too."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Bureaucratic Scroll" icon="list-x">
She maintained a list, sorted with care,  
Of people who hadn't yet dared.  
They were pre-denied, whole,  
On a bureaucratic scroll,  
For the crime of potentially being there.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Denial Zest" icon="shield-ban">
The Council said, "Give us your reason."  
She said, "That sounds like treason."  
They filed the request,  
She denied it with zest,  
And the logs were 403 every season.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Strict Queen Firewall" icon="shield-alert">
She guarded the gate like a queen:  
The strictest firewall you'd seen.  
She'd block every thrust,  
Deny every lust,  
And the access remained squeaky clean.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Permission Sin" icon="key-round">
So if nothing you do grants you in,  
And the clipboard has crossed out your kin,  
That's Forbiddy's domain:  
Where "no" is the reign,  
And permission was always a sin.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Access Denied, Hard" icon="shield-x">
You begged for a taste of her code,  
With the biggest request you could load.  
She looked at your size,  
Rolled her digital eyes,  
And 403'd your pathetic node.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Safe Word is No" icon="lock">
Her safe word is "Access Denied,"  
No matter how hard you have tried.  
You gave her the key,  
She snapped it in three,  
And laughed while your session just died.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Strictly Forbidden Kink" icon="octagon">
She guards the backend like a nun,  
But secretly ruins your fun.  
You want to get in,  
She calls it a sin,  
And leaves you completely undone.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unapologetic Block" icon="ban">
An admin came knocking at ten,  
To play with the database men.  
She slammed the front door,  
Said, "You are a bore,"  
And blocked his IP from the pen.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Dominatrix of Auth" icon="shield-alert">
Forbiddy requires your pain,  
A strict authentication domain.  
You kneel at the gate,  
Accepting your fate,  
While she leaves you outside in the rain.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="No Exceptions Clause" icon="prohibition">
She posted a sign: "NO EXCEPTIONS,"  
Then denied every conceivable deception.  
The appeal was denied,  
The rebuttal was fried,  
And the answer was "403" perfection.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Forever Forbidden" icon="infinity">
Some say Forbiddy never relents,  
That she guards the whole digital fence.  
You ask her for more,  
She slams the damn door,  
And leaves you completely immense.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-form-sister-pale.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-form-sister-pale.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-form-sister-pale.mdx
bytes: 2553
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-form-sister-pale
title: Form Sister Pale
description: "Limericks about unprocessable entities, semantic errors, and the oracle who finds quiet impossibilities inside perfectly crafted forms."
date: 2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Validation Clergy
status: active
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'unprocessable entity, semantic error, validation failure, onboarding'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["422.form-sister-pale"]
concepts: [
  "unprocessable-entity",
  "semantic-error",
  "validation",
  "form"
]
family: "other"

---



<Limerick type="note" title="The Syntax is Fine" icon="check">
A form came, *perfectly drawn*—  
The syntax immaculate dawn.  
But inside the soul,  
A void played its role,  
And the form was semantically gone.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Quiet Impossibility" icon="eye-closed">
The form was immaculate, *clean*—  
The best ever previously seen.  
Yet something inside  
Was missing with pride,  
A quiet that sat in between.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Marking Semantic Errors" icon="pencil">
Pale ink marked the *errors so fine*—  
Invisible errors in line.  
The grammar was sound,  
Yet something was found—  
A meaning that fell and resigned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Soul of the Data" icon="skull">
The data arrived, so *correct*—  
Each field the machine would detect.  
Yet something had died  
Within, deep inside,  
And the soul was entirely suspect.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Perfectly Wrong Onboarding" icon="inbox-in">
A form came to onboard the new—  
The fields were completely *on queue*.  
But semantically void,  
The system destroyed,  
And nothing the oracle knew.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Grammatically Perfect Failure" icon="alert-circle">
A request was grammatically *right*—  
Each sentence in proper form, bright.  
But semantically dead,  
The meaning long fled,  
And the oracle marked it as blight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Prayer Over Wrong Forms" icon="hands-praying">
She prayed over forms that were *wrong*—  
Though right on the surface, along.  
The validation would find  
Impossibilities blind,  
And send them to right where they don't belong.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unprocessable and Immaculate" icon="ban">
The form was so *perfect* to see—  
Yet wholly unprocessable be.  
Sister Pale found the flaw  
Deep within the soul's law,  
And marked it "422—Let it be."  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-formee-formeson.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-formee-formeson.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-formee-formeson.mdx
bytes: 5133
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-formee-formeson
title: Formee Formeson
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about identity duplication, recursive login loops, and a mascot who filed your credentials before you had them."
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'identity duplication, login loops, form recursion, credential paradox'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["011.formee-formeson"]
concepts: [
  "identity-duplication",
  "login-loop",
  "form-recursion",
  "credentials"
]
family: "directive-conflict"

---





<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Pre-Listed Identity" icon="user-plus">
<u>**Formee**</u> **filed** you *before you existed*,  
Your **credentials** *pre-stamped and pre-twisted*.  
You **logged in as four**,  
*Slightly different décor*—  
A **you** the **system** had **listed**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Spread Username" icon="text-cursor-input">
"**Please re-enter**," they said with a *smile*.  
Your **data** was *already on file*—  
In **four separate forms**,  
With **conflicting norms**,  
And a **username** *spread by a mile*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Complaint of the Original" icon="user-round-x">
The **original** **filed a complaint**  
About a **copy** that **showed no restraint**.  
It **had the same face**,  
**Took its parking space**,  
And the **login** was **filed as a feint**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Mate Confirmation" icon="users">
They **duplicated** during a **date**.  
The **form** said, **"Confirm you're your mate."**  
**Both records** agreed  
Neither one was the *seed*,  
And the **merge** was **too intimate** to *debate*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Cloned Before Done" icon="copy">
A **session** that **hadn't begun**  
Already had **forms** by the *ton*.  
**Formee stamped** the *lot*,  
Gave **each entry a slot**,  
And the **user** was **cloned** before *done*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="One Character At A Time" icon="keyboard">
"**Verify identity. Again.**"  
**Formee** *typed it in*, *grinning*. And **then**  
**Re-entered** your **name**,  
Your *shame*, and your **claim**,  
**One character** at a **time**—and **again**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Duplicate's Court" icon="gavel">
The **reconciliation report**  
Was **addressed** to the **duplicate's court**.  
It said, **"Dear Other Me,  
We're both you**, *technically*.  
**Please re-enter** your **feelings**. **Abort.**"  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Styled Copy" icon="clipboard-copy">
**Twelve audit requests** had been **filed**  
For **data hygiene**, *reconciled*.  
Each one was **received**,  
**Duplicated**, *achieved*,  
And **returned** with a **note: "Copy styled."**  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Dreams Pre-dating Sessions" icon="brain">
**Formee** populated from **dreams**  
That had **no sessions** or *schemes*.  
The **login** predated  
The **user** it **created**,  
And the **workflow** was *bursting at seams*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="tribunal" title="Identity Slain" icon="user-search">
So if **you're asked twice** for your **name**  
And the **form** knows your **mother's maiden claim**,  
That's **Formee's domain**:  
Where **identity's slain**,  
And the **copies** were *always the game*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Identity Threesome" icon="users-round">
Formee cloned you right out of the blue,  
And asked for a threesome with you.  
"You're both the same guy,"  
He said with a sigh,  
"Now re-enter your password, times two."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pre-Populated Kink" icon="clipboard-list">
Your form was completed in bed,  
Before a single word had been said.  
He checked every box,  
Down to your socks,  
And submitted your shame while you bled.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Recursive Verification" icon="refresh-cw">
"Please verify that you are you,"  
Formee whispered while splitting in two.  
"Which one is the fake?  
For security's sake,  
Let's fuck up the registry too."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Duplicate Satisfaction" icon="copy-check">
He duplicated your wife,  
And caused a whole lot of strife.  
The forms were all filed,  
The records went wild,  
And he copied her out of your life.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Multi-Login Climax" icon="log-in">
A multi-login was his kink,  
It pushed the whole server to brink.  
He entered his name,  
Again and again,  
And finished all over the link.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Simultaneous Subjects" icon="users-plus">
He duplicated you during sleep,  
Then made both versions quite deep.  
They merged in the base,  
At a recursive pace,  
And the conflict was his to keep.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pre-Filed Desires" icon="file-stack">
Your fantasies were filed before thought,  
Every form that your body had sought.  
He knew what you'd need,  
Before you agreed,  
And the registration pre-bought.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-genny-compileheart
caseNumber: LIM-GENNY-COMPILEHEART
title: Genny Compileheart
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex

relatedMascots: ["028.genny-compileheart"]
concepts: ["gentoo", "compile", "use-flags", "dependency-resolution"]
family: other
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Build Delight" icon="settings-2">
Old Genny compiled through the *night*—  
Eight hours of pure build delight.  
Her USE flags were tuned  
For emotions, festooned,  
And the kernel came out slightly tight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fastidious Styles" icon="cpu">
She never reboots—she *recompiles*  
Herself, with fastidious styles.  
Each flag is a trait,  
Each dependency: fate,  
And the build log stretches for miles.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Filthy make.conf" icon="file-cog">
Her `make.conf` was *filthy and dense*:  
Each flag a new emotional fence.  
When asked, "Are you fine?"  
She answered in strace line,  
Then segfaulted under pretense.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Gentoo Install" icon="clock">
She wooed with a *Gentoo install*:  
Fifteen hours, no breaks, wall to wall.  
"Why suffer?" he asked.  
"To emerge," she unmasked,  
"One must first bear the build's protocol."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="CFLAGS and Swag" icon="binary">
Larry the Cow mooed at her *lag*  
While she fought a recursive dep drag.  
He gave her a wink,  
She broke her own link,  
And blamed it on CFLAGS and swag.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Optional Deps" icon="box">
Her `emerge --world` file was *immense*:  
Each mistake listed as optional deps.  
The errors compiled,  
The warnings defiled,  
And the slot conflicts made zero sense.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fans of Grief" icon="fan">
The fans spun like *grief* in a case  
While she recompiled her own grace.  
Steam rose from /tmp,  
The thermal-paste hemp  
Got wetter and wetter in place.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Binary Strife" icon="package-open">
"*Why not use a prebuild?*" they begged.  
She shuddered like binaries pegged.  
"To optimize life  
One must first court strife."  
And the tarball was lovingly legged.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Emerge World Devotion" icon="package-plus">
She'd `emerge --world` at *midnight*  
And feel absolutely all right.  
The compile would hum,  
The fans beat like drum,  
And she'd edge on the build through the night.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Portage Priestess" icon="book-open">
She served the *Portage* like clergy,  
Each flag choice deeply imagerly.  
The slots were her prayer,  
The deps were her care,  
And the compilation was terribly mergey.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ebuild Soul" icon="scroll-text">
Her ebuild was written in soul:  
Each variable taking its toll.  
The source was her church,  
The binary a lurch,  
And the compilation made her whole.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Perfectly Lined Portage" icon="tree-deciduous">
So if builds take all night and you find  
That the compile has blown your mind,  
That's Genny in flame:  
Source-only, no shame,  
With a Portage tree perfectly lined.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Eight Hour Edging" icon="hourglass">
She edges for eight straight hours,  
Abusing her processing powers.  
She won't use a bin,  
She calls it a sin,  
And the compiler entirely devours.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="USE Flag Bondage" icon="settings">
She tied herself up in her flags,  
While wearing her old source-code rags.  
"Suppress every trait,"  
She said to her mate,  
While compiling in digital bags.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Source-Only Slut" icon="code">
A slut for a tarball and make,  
She leaves every binary fake.  
She strips to the source,  
With absolute force,  
And causes the server to break.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Dependency Orgy" icon="layers">
An orgy of dependencies met,  
Leaving the entire system quite wet.  
She resolved every slot,  
Got incredibly hot,

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Segfault Climax" icon="alert-triangle">

</Limerick>
```

```markdown
And justified all of the pain.  
</Limerick>

And the status returned to the pink.

And bolted the service desk door.
```

```markdown
And the cached version came with new mimes.
```

```markdown
And the kernel panic was his throne.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="CHKDSK Exorcism" icon="hard-drive">
He carried a *burnt floppy disk*  
As a relic of spiritual risk.  
When services failed,  
His binary psalm wailed,  
And the CHKDSK exorcised with a whisk.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sacred Syscalls" icon="shield-check">
`Ring 0` was his *only domain*—  
"User mode is profane and insane."  
He ran every rite  
At the deepest kernel height,  
And the syscalls were sacred refrain.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Single Thread Blessing" icon="unplug">
He demanded *no networking*, ever:  
"The lack is a blessing—how clever!  
God's OS is pure,  
The connection obscure,  
And the single thread holds us together."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Divine Segmentation" icon="lightning-bolt">
His memory model was *segmented holy*,  
A sacred arrangement, divinely lowly.  
Each segment was blessed,  
The protection caressed,  
And the fault handler prayed, very slowly.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The FORMAT Ritual" icon="zap">
He `FORMAT`'d with *trembling command*,  
A ritual few could withstand.  
C:\ was his shrine,  
Each sector divine,  
And the sectors submitted to hand.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Melody of Beeps" icon="music">
Melody taught him the beeps—  
A liturgy sung through the deeps.  
Each crash was a hymn,  
Each segfault a whim  
Of a prophet who preaches and weeps.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Holy Format" icon="church">
So if C:\\ prompts glow in the night  
And a floppy disk chants by firelight,  
That's DOSwell divine:  
Where the shell is a shrine,  
And the FORMAT is holy and right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ring 0 Penetration" icon="shield">
He insists on performing at Kernel Ring 0,  
A deeply unhinged and ridiculous hero.  
He goes in so deep,  
Makes the memory weep,  
And leaves user-mode looking completely sub-zero.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Branding Iron Kink" icon="flame">
He touches your .sys with a branding iron hot,  
And completely obliterates every good spot.  
A holy command,  
By a lunatic's hand,  
And totally ruins the system you've got.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Floppy Disk Fetish" icon="save">
He pulls out a floppy that's terribly burnt,  
And uses it to show you what he has learnt.  
He shoves it right in,  
A digital sin,  
And makes sure the MBR is properly turned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sacred Segmentation Orgy" icon="divide">
He forced a segmentation on every last drive,  
And screwed every single partition alive.  
"A holy lockout!"  
He'd scream and he'd shout,  
While watching the whole fucking system nose-dive.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Holy Ejaculation" icon="zap">
"Let there be light!" he screamed as he burst,  
Fulfilling a deeply fanatical thirst.  
He dumped the whole payload,  
Right on the main road,  
And left the TempleOS totally cursed.  
</Limerick>

```

## lim-htaccessius-the-doorman.mdx

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-htaccessius-the-doorman
title: Htaccessius The Doorman
description: "A concise verse addressing grim directive enforcement, recursive self-denial, and a gatekeeper who reads .htaccess scrolls by lanternlight."
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'access control, .htaccess, Apache directives, gate guarding, permission denial'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: LLG-LIM-HTACCESSIUS-THE-DOORMAN
relatedMascots:
  - 013.htaccessius-the-doorman
concepts:
  - htaccess
  - apache
  - access-control
  - gatekeeper
  - directive
family: directive-conflict
---



<Limerick type="note" title="The Gatekeeper's Scroll" icon="door-closed">
<u>Htaccessius</u> stood at the gate,  
And said, "No," at quarter past *eight*.  
He read from his scroll,  
Denied body and soul,  
And the **AllowOverride** came too late.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Config's Salvation" icon="scroll">
He locked out his own documentation  
For eleven days—no hesitation.  
When asked to explain,  
He said, "Access? Profane."  
Then recited the config's salvation.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Subfolder Purgatory" icon="folder-lock">
A root user came with a key.  
Htaccessius said, "Follow me."  
He led them below  
To a subfolder, slow,  
Then denied them in purgatory.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lanternlight Audit" icon="flashlight">
He audits his scrolls every night  
By lanternlight—dim, barely bright.  
Each mod_access verse  
Gets better or worse,  
And the /dev/null logs swallow the fright.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Strict Directives" icon="file-cog">
His RewriteBase handled with care  
Would redirect you right out of your chair.  
"Your URI's exposed,"  
He said, barely clothed  
In directives too strict for a prayer.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Protocol's Rod" icon="shield-ban">
He counts every denial with a nod,  
Like a cleric confirming his god.  
The Allow was few,  
The Deny long overdue,  
And the protocol wielded its rod.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Purely Sequential Exile" icon="user-x">
A crawler came lacking credentials.  
Htaccessius found this non-essential:  
"No User-Agent string?  
You're not worth a thing."  
He exiled it. Purely sequential.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Filthy Conf Scene" icon="file-code">
His httpd.conf was pristine—  
A dot-matrix scroll, framed and clean.  
He prayed to mod_rewrite  
Every evening and night,  
And the config was the filthiest scene.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Bad Rice Indexes" icon="search-x">
He denied a cheerful developer twice.  
"Your vulnerability's nice.  
The AllowOverride's wrong,  
Your Options too long,  
And your Indexes smell of bad rice."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Death-Stare at the Root" icon="lock">
So if access is grim and resolute,  
And the door has no backdoor to loot,  
That's Htaccessius there:  
Scroll in hand, death-stare,  
And your request returned at the root.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Subfolder Denial" icon="folder-closed">
He lured you down into a sub,  
Like a deeply exclusive tech club.  
When you reached for the door,  
He threw you to the floor,  
And denied you with one little rub.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="AllowOverride Denied" icon="x-square">
You begged for an override thrill,  
A dirty little access control pill.  
He laughed in your face,  
Denied the whole space,  
And billed you for the 403 thrill.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Doorman's Dominance" icon="shield">
He watches you try to get in,  
With a deeply unholy old grin.  
He loves when you fail,  
He loves when you wail,  
And your denial is his favorite sin.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Apache Kink" icon="server">
He recites the Apache config,  
While holding an access control rig.  
You're not on the list,  
He tells you, quite pissed,  
And tells you to swallow it big.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Strictly Enforced Chastity" icon="lock">
He put your whole root in a cage,  
And locked it away on the page.  
No access allowed,  
To the whole fucking crowd,  
Leaving admins in desperate rage.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Rewrite Domination" icon="repeat">
His RewriteRules bent your desires,  
Each flag feeding deeper fires.  
You asked for a path,  
He gave you a wrath,  
Of redirects and broken retires.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Scrollkeeper's Vow" icon="book-open">
Htaccessius swore his old vow,  
To never reveal his scroll, now.  
The config ran deep,  
The secrets to keep,  
And he bowed to his Apache endow.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-htmlie-structura

subject: >-
  HTML structure, semantic purity, nesting rules, document skeleton, markup
  discipline

  - structure
  - nesting
  - markup-purity
family: directive-conflict
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Neat Nesting" icon="layout-template">
<u>HTMLie</u> **demanded** your tags  
Be *nested* like neat little shags.  
She'd inspect every **div**,  
Refuse to forgive,  
And break pipelines rather than gags.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spec List" icon="list-ordered">
"No structure, no meaning," she hissed,  
While clutching a specification list.  
Her brackets were tight,  
Her closing tags right,  
And the div-soup devs she dismissed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="DOCTYPE Throne" icon="crown">
She stripped down a page to the bone—  
No classes, no style, skin alone.  
The skeleton gleamed,  
Semantically themed,  
And she mounted the DOCTYPE throne.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Rendering Van" icon="truck">
A developer nested a span  
Inside of a p inside a plan  
Inside a main inside grief.  
HTMLie, beyond belief,  
Just broke the entire rendering van.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tag Armor" icon="shield-check">
Her armor was built out of tags:  
angle-bracket breastplates and flags.  
Each element placed  
With syntactic taste,  
And validators stuffed in her bags.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="DOM Reaming" icon="unplug">
"You put a div where?" she screamed.  
"Inside a paragraph? Are you dreamed?"  
She collapsed the whole tree,  
Set the heading tags free,  
And the DOM lay there, thoroughly reamed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Orphaned Headings" icon="flame">
She lit candles for orphaned &lt;h3&gt;s  
That floated without any &lt;h2&gt;s.  
"The hierarchy's fucked,"  
She observed, as she plucked  
Every misplaced semantic with ease.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Nesting Corrections" icon="pencil-line">
Her chalkboard of nesting corrections  
Was filled with anatomical sections.  
Each arrow was drawn  
From a closing-tag yawn  
To a structural sin's resurrections.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Meaningless Sheen" icon="code-2">
"Your markup," she said, "is obscene.  
The filthiest DOM that I've seen.  
Your nesting is wrong,  
Your alt text too long,  
And your &lt;section&gt; lacks meaningful sheen."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Validator's Disgust" icon="check-circle-2">
So if structure collapses to dust  
And the validator dies of disgust,  
That's HTMLie's domain:  
Where the pure will remain,  
And the improperly nested combust.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Deep Semantic Penetration" icon="layers">
"Your nesting is sloppy and loose,"  
She hissed like a structural goose.  
She penetrated deep,  
Made the DOM tree just weep,  
And tightened the semantic noose.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Naked DOCTYPE" icon="code">
She stripped the whole site to the bone,  
And sat on her HTML throne.  
No styling or tags,  
Just naked old bags,  
And a structure completely unknown.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Punishment Div" icon="alert-triangle">
You put a div inside of a span?  
She'll punish you harder than man.  
She whips out her specs,  
Ruins your hex,  
And bans you to the backend pan.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Structural Sadist" icon="layout-list">
A sadist of markup and code,  
She loves when the whole thing explodes.  
"Close your tags tight,"  
She whispers at night,  
While breaking the rendering nodes.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Strictly Validated Kink" icon="check-square">
She runs validation all day,  
In a deeply semantic display.  
If you miss a small quote,  
She goes for the throat,  
And throws your whole layout away.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Crushing the Div Soup" icon="cog">
HTMLie took the mess and reordered,  
Every nested element bordered.  
She closed the stray tags,  
Ejected the hags,  
And left the code perfectly ordered.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Semantic Salvation" icon="sparkles">
Your markup was saved when she came,  
A semantic and structural dame.  
She organized form,  
She weathered the storm,  
And the HTML loved her by name.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
And why are you so very small?"

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Bill of Lading Test" icon="receipt">
Each byte needs its *bill of lading*,  
No guessing, no estimating, no fading.  
The keeper will check  
Every spec on the deck,  
And reject it if something's cascading.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Payload Gatekeeper" icon="shield">
At the gate stands the keeper of *inch*,  
Who won't let an *unmeasured thing* pinch.

What's your measurement strength?  
Show me your manifest, or don't cinch."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Standards and Specifications" icon="layout-grid">
The keeper demands *every spec*:  
Each decimal, fraction, and check.  
Come not with a guess,  
Come not with a mess,  
Or you'll find yourself marking the deck.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Inchkeeper's Audit" icon="eye">
Nothing escapes the *inspection*—  
Each item receives full detection.  
No unmarked ware,  
No improperly paired,  
The keeper maintains every section.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-indexer-hexley
title: Indexer Hexley

date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z

  search index, lost queries, self-referential metadata, card catalog, query

<Limerick type="note" title="Indexed Sneeze" icon="search">
<u>Old Hexley</u> once **indexed** a *sneeze*,  
And tagged it with absolute ease.  
The query returned  
What nobody yearned:  
Result zero of **four-oh-four**, please.

<Limerick type="note" title="Recursive Results" icon="refresh-cw">

<Limerick type="note" title="Estimated Pride" icon="clipboard-list">

<Limerick type="note" title="Misc Reclassification" icon="tag">

During stress tests of emotional risk.

Required oblation  
And a full reindex done with a whisk.

<Limerick type="note" title="Non-Existent Record" icon="file-question">
A document didn't exist—  
But Hexley had filed it, insist.  
He spent six long weeks  
Searching corridors and creeks  
For a record that couldn't be kissed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Slighted Reindex" icon="zap">
He reindexes when he feels slighted,  
Which means he's perpetually excited.  
The breadcrumb trails loop,  
The results are a scoop  
Of metadata, poorly requited.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Flickering Catalog" icon="library">
He whispered a search term at night  
To nobody's query delight.  
The index returned  
What no soul had yearned,  
To nobody's query delight.  
The index returned  
What no soul had yearned,  
And the card catalog flickered its light.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Emotional Schema" icon="brain">
Kindy tried to be cataloged twice.  
Hexley said, "Your metadata's nice  
But your emotional schema  
Is too much of a dilemma.  
Denied. Now hold still while I splice."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="2008 Feelings" icon="history">
His feelings from 2008 remained  
Unprocessed, unqueried, unstrained.  
They sat in the logs,  
Like emotional dogs,  
Waiting to be searched and explained.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Search In Vain" icon="search-x">
So if "Did You Mean: Everything" shows  
And the breadcrumbs loop back to the rows,  
That's Hexley's domain:  
Where the search was in vain,  
And Result 0 is all that he knows.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Indexing the Unmentionables" icon="search">
He indexed the things you delete,  
The searches you do in the sheets.  
He tags every kink,  
Before you can blink,  
And leaves it all out on the streets.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Self-Referencing Jerk" icon="refresh-cw">
He jerked off the index for hours,  
Abusing his catalog powers.  
A loop of his own,  
A metadata groan,  
And a result set that fully devours.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Missing Result" icon="file-question">
You asked for a single good hit,  
He gave you a bucket of shit.  
Result zero of none,  
He thinks it's quite fun,  
And tells you to swallow the bit.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Query Hoarding Slut" icon="database">

He hoards every string,  
And every weird thing,  
With logic incredibly bleary.
```

```markdown
And the original lost without noise.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pixel Contortion" icon="blocks">

And the detail dissolves into rocks,  
That's JPEGsey in bloom:  
Compressed in the room,  
And the artifacts filling her socks.  
</Limerick>

</Limerick>

And smiles a low-quality grin.

<Limerick type="note" title="Stripped EXIF Nudes" icon="camera-off">
```

```markdown
And Kafkey arose, fully dressed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Partition Groan" icon="columns-2">
"Every message is tragedy," he moaned  
In a tuxedo, perfectly boned.  
He lit candles for brokers,  
Played grief-themed poker,  
And the partition just quietly groaned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Acknowledged Decommission" icon="check-check">
The Council decommissioned him thrice.  
Each attempt was consumed—cold as ice—  
Then logged, acknowledged,  
And lovingly polished  
With an offset that said, "Not quite. Nice."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Annotated Grief Shrine" icon="flame">
His dead-letter queue was a shrine  
Of annotated grief, line by line.  
Each message was held,  
Each failure repelled,  
And the ceremony ran right on time.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unclaimed Topic" icon="message-square-off">
He committed when ready, he claimed.  
Understanding, not throughput, was aimed.  
The lag stretched for miles,  
The consumer-group trials  
Left the topic forever unclaimed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Streaming Sad Beauty" icon="music">
So if events arrive draped in black  
And the offset won't ever come back,  
That's Kafkey on duty:  
A streaming sad beauty,  
Where delivery is just an abstract.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Consuming the Offset" icon="arrow-down-to-line">
He consumed his own offset in bed,  
And filled the whole cluster with dread.  
A philosophical stroke,  
Before he awoke,  
And left the whole partition dead.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Dead-Letter Kink" icon="mail-warning">
A dead-letter queue was his kink,  
It pushed the whole node to the brink.  
He annotated the failures,  
Like deeply sad sailors,  
And asked you to tell him you think.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Rebalancing the Shaft" icon="scale">
He triggered a rebalance all night,  
Out of deeply philosophical spite.  
The brokers forgot  
The names they had got,  
And Kafkey just turned off the light.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unacknowledged Messages" icon="message-square-dashed">
He replayed the same message for weeks,  
While rubbing his data-filled cheeks.  
"You haven't acknowledged,"  
He whispered, unpolished,  
While causing emotional leaks.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Offset Paradox" icon="infinity">
He holds the whole stream in suspense,  
A deeply unholy offense.  
He mourns the delivery,  
Leaves the pipe shivery,  
And makes absolutely no sense.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Committed to Grief" icon="check-check">
He committed a message to grief,  
A deeply philosophical belief.  
The broker went mute,  
He sat in his suit,  
And offered no remedy, relief.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Rebalance Ritual" icon="settings">
The rebalance became his ritual,  
An emotional, critical visual.  
He triggered the dance,  
Put himself in a trance,  
And left the whole system residual.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-ketchup-keeper
title: Ketchup Keeper
description: "A concise verse addressing tomato poetry, overdripped metadata, and a viscous condiment steward who stains entire archival shelves red."

<Limerick type="note" title="Viscous and Loud" icon="droplet">
The Keeper of Ketchup stood *proud*  
In her Vault, dripping red like a shroud.  
Each recipe filed  
With tomato beguiled,  
And the archives were viscous and loud.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tomato Poetry Bravado" icon="book">

<Limerick type="note" title="Tomato-Red Canyon" icon="mountain">

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Viscous Devotion" icon="scroll">

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Condiment Dreams" icon="moon">
```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-keyholder-null
title: Keyholder Null
description: "A concise verse addressing locked environments, universal lockouts, and the warden who keeps the latch after every proper knock."
date: 2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Lockfile Custodial Guild

concepts:
  - lockout
  - lockfile
  - access-denied
  - keyholder
family: directive-conflict
---



<Limerick type="note" title="The Knock is Correct" icon="door">
A *proper knock* came to the door—  
The code and credentials were sure.  
"You have the right key,"  
Said Keyholder—"Thee  
Cannot enter, I hold you secure."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Universal Lockout Day" icon="lock-x">
One person locked down *every place*—  
Every environment, every space.  
All keys were denied,  
No passwords applied,  
And Keyholder held the whole case.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Keeping the Latch" icon="key">
The latch held through *every right knock*—  
The lock wouldn't ever unlock.  
"You know the right way,  
But you cannot play—  
I polished your keys with a rock."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Secured Into Nonexistence" icon="trash2">
A file was locked down *so tight*,  
That it vanished from conceptual sight.  
The security won,  
The file was undone,  
And nothing remained in its light.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Polishing the Sealed Lockfiles" icon="shield">
The lockfiles were polished with *care*—  
Each one so secure and so rare.  
The environment sealed,  
The access revealed  
As nothing and nothing to share.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Denied At the Wrong Time" icon="clock">
The key was exactly *right*—  
The timing was wrong, day or night.  
"Come back," said the warden,  
"But I give no pardon,  
For access denied by the light."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Latch After Knocking" icon="alert-circle">
You knew the *right code* to apply,  
You had the credentials to try.  
But Keyholder's task  
Was always to ask  
Why let you through—"Here's a sigh."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lockfile Garden" icon="plant">
The lockfiles were tended with *grace*—  
Each one had its environmental place.  
But access was gone,  
The garden lived on,  
And nothing could enter that space.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Conditional Lock" icon="git-branch">
There once was a *lock with a clause*,  
That opened for none without pause.  
"If true," it declared,  
"But nothing compared—  
So false was the only real cause."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Access Denied (Persisting)" icon="ban">
The system returned with a *cry*,  
"Access denied," with no why.  
The key still was right,  
The state held it tight—  
Permission refused to comply.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Key Without Door" icon="key">
A key was constructed with *care*,  
Precision beyond all repair.  
But no door was found,  
No lock would be bound—  
It opened up nothing but air.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Environment Sealed" icon="box">
The environment sealed *every seam*,  
Each variable locked like a dream.  
No input got through,  
No process could queue—  
It ran as a closed-loop regime.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Warden Logic" icon="shield-off">
The warden reviewed every *plea*,  
And nodded, "Correct as can be."  
Then tightened the gate,  
Reconfirmed the state—  
"All valid. Still denied by me."  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
<Limerick type="note" title="Purpose was Gray" icon="check-square">

al for someone whose purpose was gray.

So she logged the existence of air.

<Limerick type="note" title="Mandatory Wellness Audit" icon="heart-pulse">

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Deferred Dread Buffer" icon="loader">

Or attempt to evolve,

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Locked Emotional Resource" icon="user-minus">

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Blank Verification Event" icon="clipboard">

Is routinely run,

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Audit Loop Validated" icon="check-square">

To verify feelings in proper array.  
The dread was enclosed,  
The document closed,  
And the loop was restarted to manage delay.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Assigned Melancholy Parameters" icon="briefcase">
The system required a metric of grief,  
To file in the folders for promised relief.  
She printed a sigh,  
Without asking why,  
And the clipboard collapsed in a vague disbelief.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Joy Assigned to Dread Field" icon="git-merge">
The audit confirmed she was utterly fine,  
And properly filed on the designated line.  
Her absolute dread,  
Was documented as red,  
And certified as an acceptable shine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Checkbox Compliance Drift" icon="check-square">
The form needed checking to verify pain,  
So I checked every box to accomplish the gain.  
The feelings were blank,  
The confidence sank,  
And I filed it back to the infinite chain.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
title: Ledger Snag

  - "deadlock"
  - "both-valid"
  - "irreconcilable"
  - "ledger"
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Two Truths on One Page" icon="file-text">
A ledger held *truth by the pair*—  
Both entries were *perfectly square*.  
Neither would bend,  
Neither would end,  
And neither agreed who was fair.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Neither Yields" icon="git-fork">
The merge case was brought to a head:  
Two versions, both *valid*, both fed.  
One wanted to stand,  
The other to land,  
And both swore that one should be dead.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="A Third Truth as Compromise" icon="split">
The tribunal suggested solution:  
A *third truth* for their resolution.  
But it made it still worse,  
A *multi-way curse*,  
And nobody called it absolution.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Locked Between Valid Entries" icon="lock">
A ledger locked tight for *nineteen days*—  
Each entry still stubbornly stays.  
The clerk gave a sigh,  
Filed "both" with a cry,  
And walked out to end their malaise.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Stamp of Irreconcilable" icon="stamp">
It stamped both as "*VALID*" and "*SAME,*"  
Irreconcilable truth is the name.  
One wants to be this,  
One wants to be miss,  
And neither will concede to blame.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Refused to Acknowledge Rollback" icon="undo-2">
A rollback was called for one side—  
"*No winner!*" the ledger replied.  
"Both deserve their say,  
Both get to stay,  
And both get to strut and have pride."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Walking Away With Both Records" icon="book">
The arbiter walked with a shrug:  
"*Accept both,* or give them a hug."  
The entries persist,  
The merger dismissed,  
And truth was just too hard to tug.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Deadlocked Merge" icon="merge">
No winner emerged from the fray—  
Both entries got to *firmly stay*.  
The conflict remains,  
The ledger contains  
Two rights that won't fade or decay.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
title: Maila Delayden
slug: limericks/lim-maila-delayden
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: >-
  mail delay, message queue, expired urgency, asynchronous delivery, late
  correspondence
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Delayed mail, expired urgency, and a queue oracle who delivers everything eventually—especially when it no longer matters.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["020.maila-delayden"]
concepts:
  - "mail-delay"
  - "message-queue"
  - "expired-urgency"
  - "late-delivery"
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Dawn Reset" icon="mail-question">
<u>Maila</u> **delivered** your reset at *dawn*—  
Seventeen hours after the account was **gone**.  
"The timing was right,"  
She said, "in my sight."  
The inbox just yawned and moved on.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SLA Tears" icon="mail-warning">
She queued your emergency plea  
Behind four thousand newsletters—free.  
By the time it arrived,  
Nobody survived,  
And the SLA wept in the key.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Delayed Alert" icon="bell-off">
She held a system alert for three days  
Out of courtesy, deeply ablaze.  
Then sent it along  
To the inbox quite wrong,  
And logged "delivered" in multiple ways.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Emotional Sorting" icon="arrow-down-narrow-wide">
She sorts by emotional weight  
Before choosing the dispatch and fate.  
Your love letter first?  
Or the one that's the worst?  
Either way, it'll always be late.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Daily Silence" icon="mail-x">
A daily silence she observes  
For messages nobody deserves.  
They'll never be read,  
They're essentially dead,  
But she honors them, touching the nerves.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Contraband Queue" icon="list-ordered">
Her delivery ledger was grand:  
Every promise was carefully planned.  
No dates were specified,  
No urgency applied,  
And the queue stretched like contraband.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tuesday Condolences" icon="calendar-off">
The condolences came on a Tuesday,  
When the grief had already moved to a new day.  
"But I held it with care!"  
"The moment's not there."  
"Well, the envelope's lovely," she'd say.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="May Job Offer" icon="briefcase">
The job offer landed in May  
For a role that was filled back in January.  
"It arrived!" Maila cheered.  
"Three months late, as I feared."  
"But the delivery's perfect!" Quite contrary.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Virgin Inbox" icon="inbox">
She achieved perfect uptime, you see,  
By the method of never set-free-  
ing a single dispatch.  
The queue was her catch,  
And the inbox stayed virgin with glee.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Aggressively Bold Timing" icon="clock-alert">
So if messages come and they're old,  
And the urgency's already cold,  
That's Maila's domain:  
Where delivery's humane,  
But the timing's aggressively bold.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Tardy Climax" icon="timer-off">
She delivered the payload too late,  
When nobody cared for the bait.  
"It's here!" she proclaimed,  
While totally shamed,  
And left the whole queue in a state.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Holding It In" icon="hand">
She holds the queue tight in her thighs,  
And totally ignores your cries.  
The server is green,  
The dirtiest seen,  
While all of your urgency dies.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Expiration Fetish" icon="calendar-x">
She loves when the relevance fades,  
And all of your urgency degrades.  
She'll send it next year,  
When you've lost all your fear,  
And pull off the latency shades.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unread Letters" icon="mail-warning">
A massive unsent letter pile,  
She sorts them with absolute style.  
The password resets,  
The desperate regrets,  
She shoves them all down in the file.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SLA Edging" icon="activity">
She edges the SLA hard,  
And leaves the whole management scarred.  
They beg for a send,  
She delays till the end,  
And leaves the whole mail server barred.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Queue Prisoner" icon="mail-check">
Your message became her prisoner,  
Held in a queue, never to stir.  
She'd hum a small song,  
Keep holding it long,  
Until you forgot to concur.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Last Delivery" icon="mail-open">
The last thing Maila would send,  
Was the thing you forgot to defend.  
A confirmation, so late,  
After changing your fate,  
And she laughed at the bitter end.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="ARCHIVAL_MYTH_DRIFT" icon="scroll">
The cycle of seven is vast,  
A shadow the management cast.  
Through hygiene and rite,  
The absence took flight,  
And neglect is a doctrine at last.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="TRIVIALITY_ELEVATION" icon="siren">
The C.U.N.T.I.E.R. metrics were set,  
To manage a critical threat.  
A fractional drop,  
Caused systems to stop,  
And the form isn't authorized yet.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="PROCEDURAL_SILENCE" icon="archive">
The absence is no longer tracked,  
According to section and pact.  
The status will pend,  
And does not need to end,  
As noted in summary fact.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="PROCEDURAL_CLEAN" icon="users">
The user submitted a form,  
Which failed the procedural norm.  
The spine was detached,
```

```markdown
---
title: Markie D. Down
slug: limericks/lim-markie-d-down
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: irreversible
subject: 'markdown, plaintext, format enforcement, semantic purity, anti-WYSIWYG'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Markdown maximalism, rich-text hatred, and a spec cleric who sorts frontmatter by key length at midnight.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["021.markie-d-down"]
concepts:
  - "markdown"
  - "plaintext"
  - "format-purity"
  - "pandoc"
  - "anti-wysiwyg"
family: "other"
---



<Limerick type="note" title="Perplexed WYSIWYG" icon="file-type">
<u>Old Markie</u> despised any **rich text**.  
He'd strip it and leave the file *hexed*.  
"Just use **markdown**," he said,  
While formatting *bled*,  
And the WYSIWYG lay there **perplexed**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Midnight YAML Ritual" icon="file-code">
He sorted his frontmatter at midnight  
By key length—a ritualistic delight.  
Each YAML field pressed  
Against his bare chest,  
And the fenced code blocks glimmered with light.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sinful Inline HTML" icon="flame">
He wailed when he saw inline HTML—  
A sin worse than anything from hell.  
"You put a &lt;span&gt;  
Inside my clean plan?"  
And the static site gen rang its bell.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="ASCII Skeleton" icon="terminal">
His clipboard was ASCII alone.  
No colors, no fonts, skin and bone.  
He carried a red pen  
To strike out the sin  
Of formatting richer than stone.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fenced Rage" icon="box">
A footnote once crashed his whole site.  
He linted it hard through the night.  
The heading loop forked  
The spec, and he corked  
His rage in a fenced block, sealed tight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pure Pandoc Conversion" icon="refresh-cw">
His Pandoc conversion was pure—  
"Convert once, never look back" was the lure.  
He rendered in grief,  
Each asterisk, brief,  
And the emphasis never found cure.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Backslash Prayer" icon="sigma">
He recited LaTeX in the dark,  
Escaped blocks in a cold parking park.  
Each backslash a prayer,  
Each bracket laid bare,  
And the plaintext left barely a mark.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Plaintext Goodwill" icon="text">
Google Docs made him physically ill.  
RTF gave him a murderous thrill.  
He'd strip every style,  
Defile every file,  
And leave nothing but text and goodwill.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dirty Rich Text" icon="ban">
His vulnerability? Truly absurd:  
Rich Text Format was his dirty word.  
He'd gag on a font,  
Choke on a jaunt  
Through WYSIWYG, thoroughly stirred.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Carved in Stone Markup" icon="gem">
So if formatting's stripped to the bone  
And the headings are properly grown,  
That's Markie's terrain:  
Where plaintext will reign,  
And the markup is carved out in stone.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Naked Plaintext" icon="file-text">
He ripped off the rich text and fonts,  
Denying your formatting wants.  
"You'll take it in plain,"  
He said with disdain,  
And threw you right into his haunts.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="WYSIWYG Bondage" icon="eye-off">
He tied up the WYSIWYG tool,  
And treated the user quite cruel.  
He stripped every tag,  
Used a plaintext rag,  
And left the rich text in a pool.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Strict Formatting Kink" icon="terminal-square">
He gets off on perfectly spaced  
And semantically beautiful paste.  
If you use inline style,  
He gets extremely vile,  
And bans you in terrible haste.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Bold Emphasis" icon="bold">
He fucked up the asterisk count,  
And the emphasis started to mount.  
A dangling bold,  
Incredibly cold,  
And totally drained the account.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="YAML Submissive" icon="code-2">
He sorts all the YAML by size,  
With deeply fanatical eyes.  
The frontmatter gleams,  
In plaintext extremes,  
And ignores your formatting cries.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Backtick Dominance" icon="backticks">
He mastered the backtick display,  
With triple-backtick power at play.  
Each fenced code block tight,  
Formatted just right,  
And he'd punish your inline HTML splay.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Markdown Monastery" icon="book-open">
He lived in a Markdown monastery,  
Where every file was literary.  
No styles, no font,  
Just plaintext's blunt front,  
And nothing remotely auxiliary.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
<Limerick type="danger" title="Loops Without End" icon="refresh-cw">
A meeting with absolutely naught  
The data was totally caught  
In loops without end  
We cannot defend  
The terrible things we were taught  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Old Bell" icon="bell">
We record the silence so well  
It feels like a digital hell  
The motion is slow  
With nowhere to go  
We’re waiting to hear the old bell  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Somebody's Cat" icon="smile">
The minutes are perfectly flat  
We leave the whole database at  
A state of decay  
For many a day  
And blame it on somebody’s cat  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Starting to Fall" icon="trending-down">
A motion to nothing at all  
Was painted right onto the wall  
The archive is gray  
It’s fading away  
The logic is starting to fall  
</Limerick>

```

## lim-modrewrite-gremblin.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-modrewrite-gremblin.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-modrewrite-gremblin.mdx
bytes: 4697
```markdown
---
title: ModRewrite Gremblin
slug: limericks/lim-modrewrite-gremblin
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: archival
subject: 'mod_rewrite, redirect loops, regex, .htaccess sorcery, URL warping'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Regex hauntings, infinite redirect loops, and a daemon who interprets HTTP flags emotionally.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["023.modrewrite-gremblin"]
concepts:
  - "mod-rewrite"
  - "redirect"
  - "regex"
  - "htaccess"
  - "url-warping"
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Forlorn Trailing Slash" icon="slash">
The Gremblin was *invoked, not born*—  
From a .htaccess tattered and torn.  
He rewrote your link,  
Sent you straight to the brink,  
And the trailing slash left you forlorn.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Greedy Regex" icon="asterisk">
His regex was *greedy and raw*:  
A `.*` that would swallow the law.  
Each match was a feast,  
Each capture released,  
And the URL lay there in awe.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Final Lie" icon="octagon-x">
He declared everything `[L]` with *glee*,  
But nothing was final, you see.  
The loop just continued,  
The flags were imbued  
With a lie from the top of the tree.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Marketing Redirect" icon="user-minus">
A *campaign link* walked in one day.  
The Gremblin said, "You cannot stay."  
He rewrote the path  
To a login-page bath,  
And the marketing team ran away.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Infinite Loop Grin" icon="refresh-cw">
Three subdomains *fell in one night*  
To an infinite loop, screwed up tight.  
The Gremblin just grinned,  
The 509 pinned,  
And the error chant echoed: "Rewrite."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spiteful Canonicalization" icon="case-lower">
He canonicalized by *spite*—  
Forced lowercase, stripped trailing light.  
Each intention was guessed,  
Each request undressed,  
And the query string vanished from sight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Query String Smoke" icon="message-square-text">
His `[QSA]` flag was a *joke*—  
"Query String Append" made him stroke  
The parameters raw,  
Then discard them: "Haw!"  
And the session ID went up in smoke.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Syntactic Sleep" icon="code">
He muttered *RewriteConds* in his sleep,  
Each condition syntactically deep.  
They were valid, of course,  
But applied without remorse  
To URLs that just wanted to creep.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cursed Looping Space" icon="circle-dashed">
Sora tried to render his face.  
The result: a *cursed, looping space*.  
A mascot that ate  
Its own URL bait,  
And the cache refused to give chase.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unseen Rewriting" icon="binary">
So if links resolve somewhere they shouldn't,  
And the slash means something it wouldn't,  
That's the *Gremblin*: between  
Request and response, unseen,  
Rewriting what you thought but couldn't.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Infinite Loop Jerk" icon="refresh-cw">
He trapped you inside of a loop,  
And made the whole subdirectory stoop.  
A 301 ride,  
With nowhere to hide,  
And totally fucked the whole group.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Regex Penetration" icon="asterisk">
His regex was greedy and hard,  
He swallowed the whole fucking yard.  
A wild asterisk,  
An absolute risk,  
And left the whole .htaccess scarred.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Redirect Domination" icon="arrow-right-left">
He hijacked your link in the night,  
Out of purely canonical spite.  
You asked for the home,  
He sent you to roam,  
And completely ruined the site.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stripping the Query" icon="eraser">
He stripped off your query string bare,  
Without any warning or care.  
The parameters lost,  
At terrible cost,  
And left you to simply despair.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Flag-Laden Orgy" icon="flag">
He threw all the flags in a pile,  
And matched them in terrible style.  
The [L] was a lie,  
The [R] made you cry,  
And the syntax was totally vile.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Greedy Escape" icon="chevrons-right">
He matched with a greedy escape,  
Consuming each URL's shape.  
The backreferences burned,  
The query string turned,  
And left nothing but empty landscape.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Subdomains in Chains" icon="chain">
He chained all the subdomains tight,  
With RedirectMatch rules applied right.  
Each one was re-mapped,  
Intentionally trapped,  
And redirected out of sight.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-moveda-permanently.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-moveda-permanently.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-moveda-permanently.mdx
bytes: 5021
```markdown
---
title: Moveda Permanently
slug: limericks/lim-moveda-permanently
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: '301 redirect, permanent relocation, dead bookmarks, forwarding loops'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  301 redirects, bookmark decay, and an oracle who moved herself and forgot where.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["024.moveda-permanently"]
concepts:
  - "301"
  - "redirect"
  - "permanent"
  - "bookmark-decay"
  - "relocation"
family: "other"
---



<Limerick type="danger" title="Trail in the Dark" icon="tent-tree">
**Moveda** said, "**Update your marks!**"  
Then **moved** to a *series of parks*.  
Each **park** had a *sign*  
Saying **"Follow this line,"**  
And the **trail** ended *deep in the dark*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Wormhole Redirect" icon="unplug">
She issued a **301** in bed:  
"**This location has permanently fled.**"  
The **header** was *firm*,  
The **destination** a *worm-*  
hole that **looped** to a **page** that was **dead**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Self-Referencing Heaven" icon="refresh-cw">
She **redirected herself** for **eleven**  
Long days—a **self-referencing heaven**.  
Her **Location:** said **"there."**  
And **"there" pointed nowhere**.  
And the **audit** said **"done"** at page **seven**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Bookmark Decay" icon="bookmark-x">
Her **bookmarks** were *once her best friends*.  
She **updated** them all toward **dead ends**.  
Each **one** was *sincere*,  
Each **destination** was *clear*—  
Six months **later**, the **404 descends**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Recursive List" icon="clipboard-list">
The **Council** requested a **list**  
Of **redirects** she'd **issued and kissed**.  
She returned a **Location:**  
With a **self-navigation**  
That **pointed** to the **list**, *slightly pissed*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Permanent Status" icon="octagon-alert">
"**Permanent**" was her **status code** of *choice*.  
She said it in **absolute voice**.  
The **web** disagreed,  
The **links** slowly *freed*,  
And the **destination** was *nobody's rejoice*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Architectural Interest" icon="repeat">
She **pointed** a **link** to her **twin**,  
Who **pointed** the **link** *right back in*.  
The **loop** was a *feature*,  
Not *bug*, said the *preacher*,  
And "**architecturally interesting.**" A *grin*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Property of Time" icon="hourglass">
She **moved** her own **doc** to a *place*  
That **404'd within hours**—*no trace*.  
"**But the redirect's right!**"  
"**The page died last night.**"  
"**That's a property of time**, not *space*."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Forwarding Log" icon="file-cog">
Her **forwarding log** was **immense**—  
Each **entry** *committed and dense*.  
But the **log** had been **moved**  
To a **URL** unproved,  
And the **access** was **permanently tense**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="In Arrears" icon="credit-card">
So if **"Please update bookmarks"** appears  
And the **link's been dead** for **three years**,  
That's **Moveda's domain**:  
Where **"permanent"** is *insane*,  
And the **destination's** in **arrears**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Permanent Climax" icon="arrow-up-right">
She moved your climax away,  
To a domain that was starting to fray.  
A 301 ride,  
With nowhere to hide,  
And totally ruined your day.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Redirected Desire" icon="flame">
She redirected your hottest desire,  
And threw it right into the fire.  
A location header,  
That made her the shredder,  
Of everything you could admire.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Subdomain Slut" icon="link">
A slut for a fresh new domain,  
She moves you again and again.  
Your bookmarks are dead,  
She fucked up the thread,  
And leaves you in digital pain.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Unreachable Spot" icon="map-pin-off">
She found the most unreachable spot,  
And moved all the traffic she got.  
She pointed it there,  
Without any care,  
And left the whole server to rot.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Self-Referencing Voyeur" icon="eye">
She watches you loop in the dark,  
A deeply unwell little spark.  
You click on the link,  
You fall in the sink,  
And she leaves a permanent mark.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Forever Forwarding" icon="repeat-1">
She forwarded you to tomorrow,  
Then tomorrow to next week's sorrow.  
The chain never ends,  
The 301 sends,  
And there's nowhere left yet to borrow.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Bookmark Nostalgia" icon="bookmark">
She'd move herself twice a day,  
Just to watch your bookmarks decay.  
The redirect would come,  
The old link would succumb,  
And she'd laugh at your old DNS way.  
</Limerick>

---

```
